Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
59
Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Our Situation
<Prayer> Today is July 2, 1972, and it feels like just yesterday that we welcomed this year with meaning. We have already passed half a year, and this morning we are celebrating the first month of the latter half of the year, July. Among the countless Sabbaths where we have demanded the liberation and victory of all people together with the Father, I hope that today can be a day to be commemorated before Your will and before us.

Father, please protect this latter half of the year, which stands at a critical juncture where we must determine the final victory or defeat in the historical providence. We understand that life is such that it is easy to be born within limits, live within limits, and end within limits. You have started beyond this boundary and are in a position where You handle everything and affirm the goal of victory from beyond the boundary. As we reflect on this, we learn through the course of history that it is difficult for heaven and humanity to stand in a position where they can always harmonize, unite, and correspond. We are here, bowing our heads and revealing our insufficient selves before the infinite Father, so please come to us.

Throughout all historical eras, countless ancestors have yearned for the providential will and have sometimes sworn to return the final victory to heaven, and at other times have fought, but we know all too well that they have left behind many traces of sorrow rather than victory in accordance with Your providential will. Today, we are not starting from a position that transcends history; rather, we are a group that has started to overcome this within history to ultimately surpass the heights that heaven demands. Therefore, even if we pass through, as long as we do not cross the peak of the heights, we are neither this side nor that side, and we clearly understand this.

Even if we are faced with the difficult and rugged mountains, when we lament our own weaknesses in that position and refuse the environment, we come to realize that such a severe environment cannot bring us conditions for happiness. Thus, no matter how exhausted we are or how insufficient we feel, we must overcome and surpass the heights with all our lives. The destiny of restoration blocks us, and the more we think about it, the more we understand that as limited humans, it is difficult to cross that boundary.

Seeing the evil flourishing, You, Father, are pushing forward with a historical struggle to prevent and remove it. You know that this cannot be prevented by Yourself alone, and thus You have fought alongside humanity throughout history. We must understand that if it is not us, this peak cannot be crossed, and if it is not us, there is no way to set a new dividing line against evil and remove it. Therefore, we must recognize that there are individuals hidden in the path of seeking Your will who wish to overcome it regardless of the suffering they must endure.

Even if we are insignificant beings, we must realize that the Father, who embraces the heart of historical providence, desires to surpass the final peak of victory. We did not know that You, Father, are the one who comes forth with wishes for anyone. Father, now as we look at our humbled selves, we clearly see that because we started from evil, we are often evil. No matter how we look at it, internally or externally, we cannot be the nature that can seep into heaven amidst the subtlety, and no matter how much we search through the environment, we find ourselves in a position without any content that possesses Your figurative authority, blaming our insufficient selves for looking up to heaven. Father, please have mercy on us.

Yet, without these individuals, You cannot widen Your path or pass on the ties of hope. We understand the pitiful situation of the Father. We did not realize how much You have suffered before we felt our own sadness. When we see that our desire is merely to avoid hardship, we must recognize the folly of humanity that does not consider how much the Father has walked a painful path to surpass the suffering that is millions of times greater than our own.

For those of us who have experienced how difficult it is to lead a single life toward the path of salvation, we must understand how pitiful the Father's position is, who must correct the twisted and broken paths of history and ensure that anyone can envision a path of restoration as a foundation of hope and happiness. Through the history of the past, we have traversed many paths of blood and tears, and not only that, but we have also paid the price of countless sacrifices, connecting the traces of martyrdom with the miserable and tragic history that has been passed down to each of us today. We must recognize that we each hold a historical thread in our current position and that we have a responsibility to pull and carry the path of history.

We know that our own selves are not just individual beings but that history is inscribed within us. We understand that all responsibility rests on our shoulders. When we think about the path that remains for us to call upon the Father with the appearance of having won the battle that must establish goodness not only in the past and present but also in the future, we realize how sad our current position is and how much the Father's heart is tightening as He looks at us.

Father, please look upon your gathered children at this time. We must recognize that we are in a shameful position where we cannot reveal the individual 'I' before You. We did not know that our faces are shameful before You. Acknowledging that our bodies are insufficient to be revealed before the Holy Father, we admire You, the Lord of mercy and compassion, and longing for the loving Father, we entrust ourselves to You.

Although we hesitate because we are insufficient to be entrusted to You, since You are looking at us, we offer this so that it may serve as a fulfillment before Your will and as a stepping stone on the path of Your will. If there is any aspect that can be used by You, please accept it, even if it is as a pile of refuse, so that it may contribute to the growth of a single life. When the appearance of being able to offer such a pitiful heart that must receive what cannot be received manifests, we know that the Father, who possesses the power of creation, presents new ties of creation in any environment according to that heart, so please have mercy on us as we bow down despite the shame of our inadequate selves.

It is shameful that we have bowed down hoping for a shining day of glory in which we can live, but since it is the Father’s wish that anyone would avoid the place of death, we have come forth despite our nakedness and inability to hide our ugly forms, so we earnestly hope and wish that You will embrace and accept us.

Please truly open the door of Your heart and come to us with Your commands. Although we have stood in the position of coming forth for Your will until now, we must be honest before You, who knows how we have been. Not only must we be honest, but we must also be in a position where we can confess without hesitation in an automatic manner before heaven. Before goodness, we must forget ourselves, and we must become those who can have a heart that can explode with the original nature so that we can gain the Father’s sympathy, knowing that we are fallen descendants who cannot gain it without such a connection.

As You look upon these humbled appearances, if there is a wondrous glory in which You can embrace them because You love them, we earnestly hope and wish that You will remember these humble children, even if we cannot be in that position.

On this first Sabbath morning of July, may Your creative hand rest upon the hearts of each of us along with Your manifestation. May today be a morning where we can discover our shining selves that can serve as a new opportunity for tomorrow and can elevate our awareness of the heavenly ties connected to ourselves. Father, please bless us.

Father, please remember Your children scattered across the nation and Your little children spread throughout the world. There is a small group that has raised the flag of new life against the sad fate of the world, standing in a shabby appearance as frontline soldiers for heaven, so please protect them, knowing that they are the mobilization members of unification spread across the world.

Is it not our wish in the Unification Church that where You do not dwell, we do not desire to see the sacrament? Knowing that we do not want to leave anything that can remove heaven, we must realize that as long as they remain, Your will remains, and as long as they exist, Your manifestation can continue. Father, who has endured persecution, sorrow, pain, and grief, we must understand that as the time approaches when we can step over the peak of sorrow and resolve our grievances, the final desperate battle awaits us.

We are a group that has gathered to charge into this battlefield to break through and to promise a joyful day when we can leap over this peak and jump into the side of peace. Please allow glory to be absorbed along the way, allow us to represent Your manifestation in the path of struggle, and let Your glory appear with them. We earnestly hope and wish that You will work so that before all nations and peoples, we can reveal the reality of Your living power.

We know that their steps are in accordance with heaven’s command and instructions. They are not moving according to anyone’s command but are feeling the mission of the times at this critical point, and there is a procession moving in various parts of the world that feels a mission that cannot be avoided. Father, please protect them. If they are in a place to shed tears, please protect them.

When I am in such a place, I hope that You will come and comfort me. The Father who came to comfort me wishes to be with them even now. We must not become those who hope for victory centered on ourselves. We must hope for victory centered on You, and we must not become those who demand the desires of our own side. We must become a group that realizes that we must emerge only for the sake of heaven’s will.

In the position of Jesus, who prayed earnestly before the final cross on the summit of Calvary and in the Garden of Gethsemane, saying, “Not my will, but Yours be done,” may we always have a heart that can connect with that earnest heart, and may we become a group that joyfully charges forward toward the time when we can run to the Father, unite with the Father, and be absorbed into the Father.

Father, You have said that the latter half of 1972 is important. Father, who will protect this period? We know that the owner of this period is not on this earth. It is not among this people, nor is it in this world, nor can heaven take responsibility for it. We must realize that it cannot be without the insignificant group of unification, and when we think about this, we must be strong and courageous. We must stand on a firm foundation that no one can shake.

As we raise our hands and cry out to the Father, may not only heaven and earth tremble but also may the countless saints and all spirits in the spirit world cooperate. We earnestly hope that heaven can cooperate at this moment. Thus, knowing that this period must become a time to present a new initiative in a place where heaven and earth harmonize and to become the origin of a new start, Father, please guide us. Father, please protect us, and Father, please lead us to the foundation of victory.

Father, You have said that unless we become like children, we cannot enter the kingdom of heaven. Our hearts must become like children. When we think about how great the sorrow is when a child who knew the Father loses the Father, and when a child who knew the mother loses the mother, we can also think about how great the joy is when we find the lost Father and the lost mother. We must feel that the joy of finding them is greater than the sorrow of losing them, and this must be our position today.

Having been born as descendants of the fall and starting history with tears of sorrow, we lost the Father, but now, as we meet the day of reunion, it must be a day of joy where tears of gratitude can obscure our vision. We must be able to reunite with the Father along with tears that can testify to joy and victory. We must become the Father’s sons. We must become the Father’s daughters. We must also become new family members who can inherit the Father’s eternal blessings and grace, and we earnestly hope and wish that You will protect those who understand this.

Father, we are not for anyone else. We are for You, and it is not for our own nation itself but for the world that You desire, so these individuals must remain and fight. They must surely protect this land. They must surely become devoted sons and daughters who pour out their hearts on behalf of the Father. Thus, while illuminating the family, they must also become loyal subjects and virtuous women in that nation.
must become a group that realizes it cannot be without it. 
We should not lament the swift passage of time, but rather feel ashamed for not having prepared a foundation for victory before our purpose. We should not arrive at this place, weary and despairing without hope for tomorrow, calling out to you with a heart that cries out in anguish. Instead, no matter how many times we fall, we should hold onto the hope of tomorrow and comfort ourselves by saying, "Father, please endure." We must realize how precious it is to struggle to overcome our current situation without seeking your cooperation.

14 Our Situation
We dedicate everything we have fully before you, Father, so please protect us. We do not need many words. What we need is the longing to see you and the deep feelings in our hearts. When we meet you, we should have a strong desire to hear your story rather than our own. The essence of a believer is to feel a deep yearning to become a sacrifice on behalf of their brothers, and we must realize that we are to become the pioneers among those you seek.

No matter how naked we may be, that shame will be covered there, and no matter how urgent and lacking we may feel, we can take pride in being protected in the presence of your glory, which lacks nothing. As we come to understand that we can participate in your glory from a position that is not one of deficiency, we earnestly hope that you will remember this group that has come here this morning.

If there are those among your children scattered across the nation who are longing for this place, earnestly desiring it and shedding tears, Father, please do not pass them by. Go to them, comfort them, protect them, and bless them a millionfold, we earnestly ask.

Now, please personally oversee everything that remains. We dedicate this month before you, so please take it, and we offer our understanding before you, so please take it. We earnestly request that it may be a month that can be remembered, and we present all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> You all take pride in being members of the Unification Church. We also take pride in the fact that our Unification Church is an organization that represents the purpose. We take pride in the fact that this Korea, where our Unification Church exists, is the nation that inherits the purpose. We also take pride in the fact that this era can shine in history.

All beings exist because of God.
This position we find ourselves in as the Unification Church, or as ourselves, is not something we have created. Our position in this era has also been established by God, and we must understand that this country is in this position as part of God's providence. Furthermore, the Unification Church has not established this foundation by itself, but it is known that God is the motivation behind our current situation. You may think that you have become a member of the Unification Church because you wanted to stand in such a position, but we must recognize that this is not the case.

The place where I exist and the connections I have are not created by me. The Unification Church did not come into being because of itself. Korea has not reached this providential position because it wanted to. The time for this era to fulfill a historical mission has not come because this era demanded it. We must understand that everything has come to be because of God, who is behind it all. In other words, we must recognize that the position we find ourselves in was not created by us.

I was not born because of myself. Men were not born for men. Were they not born for women? Women were not born for men? When we consider the fact that these roles exist to affirm the value of relative purposes, we see that men were born for women, and women were born for men.

Then for whom were people born? Were people born for people? Human beings are ultimately resultant beings, and for that result to manifest, there must be a motivating cause. Therefore, there must be a subject that serves as the motivation for that birth. This is undeniable.

When we look at our bodies, our eyes were not created for the sake of eyes. They were created for the body, right? Hands were not created for the sake of hands, but for the body. All limbs exist for the sake of a greater whole. This is a natural principle.

When we view it this way, the Unification Church was not created for the sake of the Unification Church. It was first created for God. Then it was created for this country and this world.

Today, our country or this world has not come into being because they wanted to. They have come into being centered around God, who is behind it all. Therefore, in order to connect the relationships behind it in a more valuable way, to create something more valuable, and to determine a place of greater shining value, there must be something that takes on the role of a principal factor.

There will be individuals and organizations. That organization, whether it be a nation or a people, must take on a leading role. When that leading role is fully realized, the nation will stand on a certain purpose standard, and centered on that purpose standard, there will be a new leading role on the global stage of a new generation, where hope can be instilled in humanity. This is an undeniable fact.

When we see this, we must understand that my current position and my existence are not created by me. You must understand this.

You may think that the 50 years I have lived, or the life journey you have lived, are yours, but they are not. You must recognize that there was a motivation behind your life that allowed you to live in such a way. When one forgets this background, they feel isolated. They feel emptiness.

When one pursues subjective responsibility within themselves and desires to start a new path based solely on themselves, they always become weak. They find themselves in a lonely position. However, when I realize that I am in this position not because of myself, but because of a great historical motivation, a providential motivation, or if God is there, then because of God, I become strong. This is necessary. This is strong before it collapses. Isn't it the same for people? When one has strong support behind them, they become strong.

Today, those who escape from this evil world, who take the conditions of their environment as a fence or a foundation larger than themselves, are strong. When one steps out alone without this, it is extremely dangerous. They are alone. When a small number of troops face a vast army in battle, their lives may be at stake, but if they know that stronger reinforcements are advancing behind them, they will seek strategies to maintain their position, no matter how difficult it may be, and will surely devise strategies to prolong the battle amidst difficult confrontations. They do not approach the battle from the perspective of a loser, but rather from the hopeful perspective of a future victor.

When we consider this issue, today, we think that we have started alone. Isn't this a shortcoming of a believer? You must understand that thinking you are doing all of this by yourself is foolish.

Today, I have become what I am because history has mobilized to present me as evidence. Those who discover their identity as evidence presented are formidable individuals. When one realizes their position, the greater the background, the stronger and more resilient they become. Those who feel the historical awareness and the awareness of the origins of their existence before their own self-awareness are great individuals. Ordinary people do not wish to stand in such a position. It is difficult to stand in such an aware position, but when one feels that and steps forward with self-awareness, they are no longer an individual.

If God exists, that God is not just the God who exists at this moment. He is not the God who can always relate to my emotional state. That God is the God who has existed from the past to the present, the historical God. Therefore, the path that God has looked upon while carrying on history is not through those who are caught up in their own self-awareness and efforts. The direction of history that can be connected is one where God develops providence through the lifestyle of a person who stands in an aware position centered on their self-awareness and who understands the content of providence. This must be seen as a public position, not a personal one.

When I stand as a qualified individual in place of that guaranteed environment, the more I feel the value behind it, the more I can conquer and overcome any enemy, no matter how strong they may be. This is an automatic principle. It is not about overcoming with someone else's support, but rather overcoming from an autonomous position.

If your conviction does not come first, you will not succeed in anything. Moreover, if you have already lost your fighting spirit, you will not be able to approach the battle with the right stance and will become a loser. Then where does that fighting spirit and confidence come from? It is impossible to derive it from oneself. Therefore, the more a nation with purpose and a high level of civilization feels the stimulus that "our historical ancestors have established this tradition," the more necessary it is. "We are standing at the moment to inherit that tradition. We have reached a moment when history can shine brighter. To resolve that, I will strike and present an action. This action represents history." A group that steps forward with a resolution filled with this conviction is strong.

You must be able to see the whole through the individual.
When we quietly observe the members of the Unification Church today, they are all walking alone. Alone. Do not think you are alone. You have learned through the principle that "we humans are microcosms. Humans have both internal and external forms and characteristics. This is true through God's nature and all external symbolic elements. We are the common elements of all things." Humans are like microcosms.

Then, does a person standing alone represent only their own history of 20 years? No, they represent the entire history since the creation of humanity. The movements of that one person represent the movements of the universe. A person who stands with this awareness of their background is dignified.

When Jesus said, "What does it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses his own soul?" he was not referring to the life of an individual within 30 years. He was speaking of a hopeful life that can govern the universe. A person who stands with this awareness, along with a greater relational background, is a strong person. One must be strong to win in battle.

In the balance of power, the weaker side loses in battle, while the stronger side wins. Victory and defeat are determined by the differences in superiority. What determines that superiority? Is it because one’s body is large? Is it because one is strong? No. If there is a person who can represent the subjectivity of the connected origins, God will leave that person to emerge.

Today, being a member of the Unification Church means being an exhibit of the Unification Church. No matter how hidden a piece may be in an exhibition, it has its own dignified history. It has the qualification to participate in that exhibition, possessing something dignified in its own right. If it is placed in a prominent position, it has gone through an average connection in its internal relationships, which allows it to appear as an exhibit.

When we view it this way, today’s members of the Unification Church are not just members for the sake of being members. They must be members who represent the Unification Church as exhibits. Therefore, when we examine them, we should be able to understand the present state of the Unification Church through them. We must be able to understand it clearly. Through their daily lives, we should be able to see the current state of the Unification Church. Only then will they remain long with the fate of the Unification Church. Furthermore, when we examine them, we should be able to glimpse not only the present but also the history of the Unification Church. This is necessary.

The Unification Church was not born for itself but was born through deeper internal connections. The deep place in the history of the Unification Church is for the sake of the nation. That nation is for the world, the world is for God, and that God is… God is mobilized for love. Therefore, we must draw upon the greatest love of God and invest ourselves in the position of serving the world. This is the position that individuals must take from the perspective of providence.

Thus, whether it is an advanced country or the United States, what is the difference between the citizens of those countries and our own? When we eat, we eat more. You see, the United States is a land of freedom, but go see that society. We think we are a land of freedom and openness, but the people living there are completely restricted. They do not know how to break the law. If you draw a line and say that today, instead of going west, they should go east, those who were going west will go east. It is not that they go because someone is there or do not go because someone is not there. They go regardless of whether someone is there or not. That is why they are a highly civilized people. They are citizens of an advanced nation. In some ways, this is a lack of freedom. It is not freedom.

Because that nation is one that can protect and nurture the traditional connections that can be roughened at any time, that nation can guarantee history. Because it can guarantee history, it can emerge as a qualified individual in the present. Those who cannot guarantee history are failures and destroyers of the present. How can we know this? We can know it through the lifestyle system. Those who stand in a position to guarantee and manage history will ultimately…
people are known for their culture, history, and values. 

As a citizen of an advanced nation, one can glimpse into that country by observing just one person. Similarly, by observing one member of our Unification Church, one can gain insight into the entire church. Such a person, no matter how much they may fail, does not perish along with their individuality. Even if they fall, they do not fall alone; they fall with the Unification Church. Whether they live or die, they do so with the Unification Church. This is how it works.

What is a patriot? A patriot is someone who lives not for themselves but for their country. A true patriot does not die alone; they die with their country, and whether they live or die, they do so with their country. This is an undeniable fact. This is the reality.

Do not think about your own situation. 

When viewed this way, you are always living bound by your own concepts, your own ideas. This is the enemy. What is the motivation for the fall? The fall began from a self-centered awareness. Isn’t that so? Eve desired good things. She thought she should become like God. This was the bait that Satan used. The origin of evil lies in the inability to transcend the boundaries created by a self-centered awareness.

Therefore, a person with a strong sense of self-awareness is inevitably lonely. They are lonely. No matter where they go, they are alone. The more they act, the more they do not expand; instead, they become narrower. Do you know what a whirlpool is? At first, it spins in a circular motion, but as it moves, it does not widen; rather, it tightens. The back becomes the front, and the back becomes the front again, tightening until it becomes a whirlpool. When it becomes a whirlpool, it sucks everything in. We see that it tries to follow a different path.

When we seek to be liberated from the whirlpool of death, we must understand how the whirlpool of death came to be. It originated from a self-centered awareness. Adam began to spin away from Eve, and Eve began to spin away from the archangel, creating a curve that spun without a center and eventually fell away. This must be liberated. 

For our situation, we must not start from a self-centered awareness. Since humanity originated from a self-centered awareness, any restoration or salvation that starts from that place cannot succeed.

So what should we do? What should we be aware of here? We must urge a historical awareness. When we say, "It is historical. It is historical," we are ultimately addressing the fundamental issue. It is an awareness of a true person. What is the true meditation spoken of in Buddhism? It is an awareness of the mind. So where does that aware mind come from? It does not come from the mind itself. It begins to exist from the foundational origin of its essence. Once we become aware of the fundamental nature of the mind, we realize we are not alone. When we discover the subject, we are not there for anyone else; we enter a state of awareness that is for the subject. When we become one, transcendent power can shine forth.

That is why someone like Buddha could confidently say, "I alone am the honored one in heaven and on earth." History exists to form that one valuable existence, so when we appear in that position, history must exist because of it. That is why he could boldly say "I alone am the honored one."

Therefore, what Unification Church members must always think about today is to not think about their own situation. They must revolutionize their thoughts about their current position. "What is my current position...?" This must be revolutionized. Whether it is Kim or Park, they must abolish their own identity. God operates in such a way. You see, anyone who has even a slight mystical experience knows this immediately. What they wish to love, God completely shatters.

God's providence unfolds gradually and imperceptibly.

When we look at the life of our teacher, he cut off even the friends he trusted the most. There are no exceptions. If he trusts a family, but that family does not align with the will and cannot be of help in the future, he will dismantle it. This applies to individuals as well as families. If any organization is not suitable, it will be dismantled. If any nation is not suitable, that nation will also be dismantled. The nation may take a long time to dismantle due to its size, but the fundamental principle remains the same. Why does it get dismantled? Because it becomes an obstacle. If God is present, He must remove that obstacle.

Today, why has the established church weakened despite opposing the Unification Church? It is because of the Unification Church. In opposition, one must absorb the other, and one must be absorbed. Otherwise, unity cannot occur. It cannot develop further. Development lies in the complete absorption of both into one before God. If there is a natural absorption without contradictions or conflicts, rapid development occurs. However, if the absorption takes place in an unnatural environment, the development will be slow. This is the principle.

Until now, you have thought, "Oh, my current position. If it is invaded, it will be a big problem." You believe it begins and ends with you. No, that is merely a point in the flow of history. It is just a point.

In terms of mountain ranges, no matter how far they stretch, they must have a significant peak connected to shine and glow. Similarly, humanity may not know, but from God's perspective, looking at numerous nations or peoples is like viewing mountain ranges. A mountain range like the Himalayas, majestic and grand, becomes an object of reverence in the world. The fate of a nation is the same.

Even if a flat plain starts beautifully, it eventually ends up in a swamp. No matter how good the beginning is, that is how it goes. When you look at Hallasan, at first glance, it does not appear that high. It seems smaller than your height. Why? Because the slope gradually increases, you do not realize how high it is. However, when you climb it, you sweat. It looks the same as you go, but when you look back, you realize you have climbed a lot.

Our Unification Church is on a similar path. It is tedious. It is boring. Oh, whether it is the will or anything else, it would be nice if something drastic happened, like a sudden illness or injury, but every day is the same. There is no change, but if you keep walking the path of ascent, you will surely discover a significant difference between yesterday's self and today's self.

God's restoration providence is not about temporarily destroying the world. It is gradually overcoming without anyone knowing. You must understand this. It is like a surprise attack. You know the term "surprise attack," right? Trying to decide victory or defeat immediately is a surprise operation, and that is inevitable. A surprise operation is a goblin-like tactic. However, when an elite army operates, it is a normal operation, so they know everything from training to the operation itself. They know from the moment they start. They know, but it is a regular war. However, it does not mean defeat; it means gradually winning. Gradually winning ensures that even in a ruined position, there are no adverse effects. Do you understand what I mean? If you engage in fierce battles and win to seize the spoils, there will be nothing usable. If you win gradually, the seized items can be completely utilized. You must understand this.

God does not use goblin tactics. He conducts long-term operations, long-term operations. You may not even realize when He wins. He wins during periods of sleep and rest. That is why even if you lose, you do not realize you have lost. You must understand this. If you have spent ten years in the Unification Church, you should ask yourself, "How much have I worked for the Unification Church during that time? Have I contributed anything significant?" When you look closely, you find nothing. It may seem like there is nothing, but the Unification Church has developed.

The higher the summit of a mountain, the more people do not increase. As the summit approaches, the number of people who follow and climb decreases. Do you understand what I mean? This is how it is. Who crosses the treacherous summit first? It is not that ten people line up and say, "Let's go!" and cross together. It is someone who crosses alone. The more treacherous the mountain, the more likely it is that someone crosses alone.

<Words> There is no one who does not know about providence in the life of faith.

Happiness comes when the cause and effect, subject and object are completely united. 
Whether we look at the created world or at historical humans, they are undoubtedly products of results. 
They are products of results. For a result to appear, it must go through a process caused by a cause. 
Without that, a result cannot be formed. When a result belongs to a higher dimension of cause, 
that result can pursue a more valuable purpose. However, when a cause that is in a higher dimension 
takes a direction that diverges from the result, it cannot meet the result that the cause pursues. 
The cause must take a unified direction toward the result it pursues, and when it deviates from that, 
it is a natural conclusion that the result cannot align with the cause. Therefore, in cause and effect, 
there is a process, and in that process, there can only be one direction, not two.
When we see this, we realize that today, we humans are not causal beings. 
If we were a complete causal being, it should be able to immediately occupy a complete result. 
Only then can a complete cause and a complete result unify into one at once, and from there, complete joy 
is formed. We know that complete joy cannot be formed by leaning to one side. When two people meet 
and speak, when the person called "A" speaks, if the person called "B" completely unites with that, 
both the speaker and the listener are joyful. Happiness cannot be formed in a solitary position. 
There is only happiness when the cause and effect, or subject and object, completely unite.
From this perspective, when we look at the causes and effects of all existence, 
there must be a direction that can connect to the cause, and there must be a direction toward the result. 
Therefore, when we look at humanity itself, if humanity is in the position of a complete result,

For example, if we talk about the fruit of a tree, when that fruit is a perfect fruit, the fruit harvested

That is a harvested result, but it is not just a result that has been harvested; it cannot escape the relationships

The conditions for the existence of all beings and the principles of action
When we look at this natural world today, every existence in the natural world, to borrow the terminology of our principles, has a nature and a form. The nature and form are internal and external; the external exists for the sake of the internal. What is the internal for? It is not for the sake of the internal but for the sake of the external. What exists is not for the current position but for something better. To become something better cannot happen just in that place. It must go through some process to be achieved.

When we see it this way, if our human happiness started from the time of the ancestors Adam and Eve, would it be for their happiness alone? It should not be just for their happiness. It speaks of another central being.

We can see that the world of all things is the same. Looking at the natural world, nothing exists independently. Everything exists and endures in relation to others. Even the smallest animals or the elements of the mineral world must pursue relative relationships to gain strength and act. It is universally acknowledged that to exist, one must have power. "To exist, one must have power. One must move." This is what is said. It cannot be denied. The composition of this universe is due to power.

Then how is power itself formed? Power cannot arise without action. To act, what must happen? Can one act independently? There is nothing that acts independently. This can be clearly felt in the world of science, especially in a chemistry laboratory. No matter how much effort the experimenter puts into causing some action through certain elements, it cannot be done with human power alone. There are elements that cannot be manipulated in that way.

Why is that? Because the relative conditions have not been established, no matter how much power a person adds, it cannot happen. Action occurs only when another force is established that can amplify the ideal power constituting that element, but it is impossible in a situation that acknowledges the existence of that element's power. When relative conditions are not established, no matter how much one tries to act, it cannot happen. It is impossible. However, when relative conditions are established, action occurs naturally without any effort. No matter how much one tries to refrain from it, it happens. This is the law of nature.

From this perspective, when we delve into fundamental issues, we see that everything that exists cannot endure without the conditions of subject and object, and there is no principle of the universe that acts to incur loss in the action of subject and object. We can conclude this. There is no action that is done to incur loss. No one engages in business to incur a loss. If you came to the Unification Church this morning to incur a loss, that person is not normal. It is the heavenly law that one acts in pursuit of gain. This is the principle of the universe.

Development occurs when the subject and object can reach a better dimension
If we acknowledge this principle, evolutionism will become a problem. Furthermore, when we establish this principle, the dialectic, which has become a global issue as a so-called communist philosophy today, will also become a problem. The idea that opposing entities struggle against each other in a conflicting position to develop does not align with the principles of heavenly law.

When we look at force in dynamics, there is no law that the incoming force and outgoing force are the same. When some action is taken, the outgoing force must always be smaller than the incoming force. Input cannot equal output. The output is smaller than the input. From this perspective, how does an amoeba act and produce something larger? This becomes a question. How can it emerge? To emerge, two factors are necessary. Does the amoeba have the subjective creative ability to create something larger than itself? If not, does it have the inductive power to draw strength from elsewhere? These two factors are necessary. Without these two factors, development cannot occur.

Then where does development take place? Development is only possible when the environment of relative conditions is established, and both can become more positive, where both negatives and positives can become positives, allowing the two to reach a better dimension. This is the logic that the Unification Church advocates today.

The cross of Jesus 
Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." Did he pray well or poorly? I think he prayed well. Do you think he prayed poorly? "He prayed poorly." Why poorly? Should it have been, "Ah, let your will be set aside and let my will be done"? No, it should have been, "Your will is my will, and my will is your will." He should have prayed like this. 
Why did Jesus pray like that? There must have been a certain pattern of disciples that Jesus desired. And there must have been a pattern of what it means to be a follower of Jesus. There must have been, right? When the promised Messiah was to be sent, there must have been a pattern for Judaism on how to welcome the Messiah. If the Judaism that Jesus envisioned and the Israel he envisioned had completely united inside and out, what would have happened? God promised to send the Messiah for the sake of the Israel nation and Judaism thousands of years ago. If the people and the church who received that promise had united according to God's will, would Jesus have prayed like that? "Your will is my will, and my will is your will. I have a responsibility to lead the church you established well, and I must govern the nation you established well, right?" He should have prayed like that. But because the nation and the church were out of alignment with the position God wanted to guide, when he tried to take the nation and the church, he was in conflict with God, and when he tried to follow God, he was in conflict with the nation and the church. Therefore, Jesus was in a position where he could not help but follow God, even if it meant abandoning the church and the nation of Israel. Isn't that why Jesus is a pitiful figure? 
Jesus did not come to die. He did not come as a coward to fall helplessly. He should have been in an environment that was sufficient to mobilize Israel and the Arab nations, blessed as the twelve tribes descended from Abraham, to oppose the mighty Roman Empire. At that time, wasn't the political climate of Rome weakened? You must understand that. 
What should the Israel nation that God was looking for have been like? What should the Judaism that God was looking for have been like? Pilate wanted to save him, but who said, "Let Barabbas go, and let us kill Jesus. Let us crucify Jesus"? It was the Jewish people. In this way, Jesus also looked at the world connected to the Israelite nation and Judaism, which was bound to perish on the cross, and said, "If you forgive me, even if I die, please forgive them, and if you want to send me, please send me back to the Israel nation that came first." Even while dying, he prayed for blessings for his enemies. "God who has forgiven me, if you have love, please forgive them through me." Did not this idea of prayer become the motive for the extension of the path to save the world today? We must understand that.  
Thus, we need someone who can represent individuals, families, ethnicities, nations, and the world. Even if there are ten people, it cannot be done; it must be through one person. Because God is an absolute God, it is a principle that the absolute God must start through an absolute individual, isn't it? However, since there is no such person in the human world, He has said He will send His beloved son again.  
The Unification Church must urge global reawakening  
Therefore, there is the idea of the Second Coming in religion. When the Lord comes and presents the covenant of judgment, it is not to bring destruction. An individual must be praised along with their family, praised through their tribe and nation, praised through the state and the world, and when God strikes the opposing group, there must be someone who can say, "If you forgive me, please forgive them." Is there a religion today that can do that, or are there religious people with such faith? No, there are not. Because there are none, it is bound to perish.

We are not trying to unify through force or violence, but through heart. We must delve into the heart of the Father, who cries out to find the heart of the individual, saying, "Isn't this the son and daughter you wanted to meet? Isn't this the repented son? Standing at the crossroad of providence, we must completely separate ourselves to the right. We must separate the new heaven, new nation, and new individual. My individual stands for heaven and for the nation. The nation and heaven stand for my individual. The nation stands for the world. Do you understand? You must understand that. Of course, the nation stands for the people, but if it stands only for the people, it will perish. Only when it can serve the world can it serve the people, and only then can the people become a people who inherit the world. Thus, we have gone through the era of individualism to the era of familyism, from familyism to tribalism, nationalism, and statism, and now we are in the era of globalism. As we go through this, the era of globalism will also pass, and ultimately, at the end of globalism, what era will come? It will be the era of Godism. This is how it ultimately returns.  
To know God's heart, one must live a life of love  
So what is Unification Churchism? It is Godism. This is how we see it. Godism, through that perspective, can resonate with anyone. It is not about serving an abstract God, but about serving a living God. In the Unification Church, we discuss God's heart.  
Today, when we speak of "theology," theology is about learning God. However, knowing through learning does not mean knowing the heart. You must understand that. Knowing does not mean knowing the heart. "That person is Reverend Moon. I see how his eyes look, how his nose looks, and how he appears." Knowing like this does not mean knowing oneself. Therefore, one must live with that person. Do you understand? No matter how wonderful someone is, when you live with them, all the excess will be revealed. Isn't that so? "Yes." You must live with them. Living does not mean living blindly; you must live well. How do you live well? You must live with love. That is how it becomes.  
You must live through love. You must live a life of love. Therefore, when God is sad, I feel that sadness, and when God is happy, I unknowingly become happy. What does a filial child do? Even if they are ten thousand miles away, the love of the parents is always with that filial child. Do you understand? In God's omnipresence, where is God? It is not in knowledge. Knowledge, the essence of individual truth, ends with that as a causal motivation, pursuing that form, that is, seeking the second generation in the opposing world. However, love is different. It is the heart of a parent who loves their child, transcending extremes and making omnipresence possible. Isn't that the heart of a parent towards their child? Isn't it? In that path of love, parents are omnipresent. There is nowhere they are not. That is only possible through love. Only love can completely dominate that child. Isn't that so? The omnipotent authority corresponds to that.  
That is how it is.  
Therefore, knowing God is not just about knowing, but about living with God. What did God want to do by educating humans? It was not just to make their heads bigger. After teaching them, He wants them to act. He wants them to live together. What does He want them to do while living? Does He want them to cry, or does He want them to rejoice? He wants them to rejoice. To rejoice, they must love.  
We are moving towards such a place.  
Then how do you feel God's omnipresence? Feel the air as God's breath, and when a storm comes, feel it as God's exhalation. When there is flowing water, feel it as the sweat God shed while overcoming the path of suffering for this world. When you look at the sun, know that it symbolizes the life force of the entire universe, and learn God's love from the sun. In understanding God's heart, nature is a textbook and teaching material established to make beloved sons and daughters happy, isn't it? That is true.  
If there is someone who can look at a leaf and regard it as their own son or daughter, and mutter to themselves, that person is close to being a saint. Do you understand? They are not crazy.  
Where is happiness? If it is in knowledge, then go seek that knowledge. Where is happiness? It is in love. Isn't that so? "Faith, hope, and love, these three remain, but the greatest of these is love." Love has infinite omnipresence. Love has infinite permanence. Love has infinite potential. Infinite vitality is established there. To achieve great purposes with great hopes, temporal distance is necessary. However, to go through that process, to pursue the day when that process can achieve a greater purpose, progressive stimulation must be sought according to time. Where do we receive that stimulation? From knowledge? Not a chance. Knowledge ends when it concludes, "That's it." Only love…  
Subjective love can take without losing its center  
You must think of the son who can receive God's love, representing the universe. Even when eating, even when alone, can you see God? You cannot see Him. How do you realize that? All things in this universe possess all of God's attributes. They are symbolically drawn to represent God. It is like a canvas. Looking at it, taking it in, and feeling joy… Isn't that so?  
If someone is captivated by their own artwork, day and night, looking at it and shedding tears of admiration, would the artist feel bad about it? "Why is this person crying?" Would they say that? If there is such a person, they would bring them in and say, "Why did you do that?" and let them tell their story, wouldn't they? "Oh, how wonderful, oh, how I miss it, oh, how I want to be together." Would they say they are crazy for that? Even if you do not know God, because God exists in the omnipresence of the universe as a loving being rather than as an intellectual subject, it is in that place of "How can I feel the resonance of love across various fields, transcending nations and through the world?" that God is re-recognized.  
Thus, when you come out with the conviction that you stand in the position based on God's love, that love is not personal love. It is subjective love. Therefore, it is not transactional love where you give to someone and remember, "Hey, I gave this to you." It is not a business-like love where you expect something in return. "Since I gave a hundred, you should give me a hundred and one." It is love that feels embarrassed after giving. You must feel embarrassed after giving.
Parents, no matter how good clothes they provide for their beloved children, will still think, 'Did not countless princes and princesses come and go on this earth? Is my son any less than those princes? Is my daughter any less than those princesses?' Thus, they have a desire to love even more. Therefore, when they think of the clothes they provided in such a context, the heart of a parent who wants to love more than anyone else in the world, more than any son in the world, is in a position where tears precede them in order to provide even better clothes. For such parents, no matter how much their son digs deeper, there is no end.

That is why, at that point, love is finally taken. If there is an end, it is not taken. It does not get taken after one round. It gets taken when one loses their center after going around several times. We must engage in love that is taken.

That is why there is love that can be given and forgotten, that is, love that does not record in a notebook that I have given, and love that does not have the mindset of receiving after giving, but rather has the mindset that it is better to have given than to have received when the other party is grateful. When both the giver feels sorry and the receiver feels sorry, that love remains forever. It should not be, 'Oh, that was my feeling,' and then afterward, 'It’s gone.' The love should not disappear even after they have exchanged. They should become such an ideal couple.

However, if the wife loves the husband and the husband loves the wife, and then one says, 'Oh, you should love me more than I love you,' that is a love that can be destroyed. Even after loving, if one says, 'I am still lacking. I am still insufficient,' this kind of love should become a foundation, and that should be the basis from which good fruit can be harvested, and a foundation can remain. Only then can an ideal family be formed, and the nation can be sought and found. Do you understand? "Yes."

Goodness is for the whole 
So what is goodness? Goodness cannot be established by serving oneself. It is established by serving others. There is no goodness in serving oneself; goodness exists in serving others. God also created the heavens and the earth day by day and looked at all creation, saying, "It is good." Where does that goodness begin? It is not that I am good when I am alone. It is from the position of having created relative beings, looking at those beings, and having the attitude of caring for them, that a historical tradition of goodness has been established. Historically, we cannot deny that the origin of goodness is not in serving oneself but in serving others. 
When we say that a person is good, what kind of person is that? It is not someone who moves to digest the environment for their own sake, but someone who has digested themselves and moved the environment. Such a person is undoubtedly a good person. 
Buddhists often talk about doing good deeds and compassion. In other words, they say to accumulate goodness, which means that goodness is accumulated by making merits for others. 
When goodness is fully accumulated and achieved, it stands in a position that is neither for the other nor for the subject. When a couple becomes completely one and achieves a united heart, that couple is not solely for the husband or solely for the wife. When a united heart is achieved, whose is it? It belongs to the couple. This is how it works. At the same time, whose is that couple? It is public. When we say that a couple has become one, it is neither the husband's nor the wife's. It is public. 
What does public mean? It means that when a certain environment combines the subject and the central content, and when that center moves in complete harmony, a foundation of goodness is established there. This is how it works. When A and B become one, they may have become one because of the existence of A or the existence of B, but it is neither A's nor B's. It must belong to both. The goodness that belongs to both is not just theirs. It represents the whole and is the whole. We must understand this. 
Where does happiness come from? Where is complete happiness established? Happiness is not established by me being happy alone. Happiness is established when both are happy. What does it mean for both to be happy? It means being able to connect to a higher level of relationship. If A comes from the east and B comes from the west, then the east and west connect. When this happens, happiness unfolds. When this happens, complete goodness is determined. 
When complete goodness is determined, one feels a complete sense of happiness. Why is that? It is because it is the time when numerous historical events that have formed relationships according to connections finally bloom. When viewed through such connections, it is the resurrection of connections, and when viewed through relationships, it appears as a single fruit. Therefore, we cannot help but see that place as a happy place and a good place. 
The foundation of compassion and love is established when the subject gives to the object.

The thought of the Unification Church is theism.

Today, our Unification Church thought is theism. The term theism is interesting. What is theism? It is the house, the home. Theism is the doctrine of God's house. Why is a house good? A person without a home is a pitiful person. A person without a home has no hometown. Isn't that right? A house is where I was born, where I grew up, where I live, and where I die. Isn't that so? It is structured that way.

From the beginning of life, whether one lives well or poorly, all connections are resolved here, and everything is displayed, and in the end, one packs their belongings and goes to that house. They cry when they are born in that house, and they must go from that house, whether they cry or laugh. The place that can finally conclude all beginnings and ends is the house. Isn't that right? That is why the house is good.

Until now, what has that house become? It has become a house without God. It has become a house without a master. That is why it is a fallen world. It is not a house centered on God, but a house centered on individuals. It has become a house with the name Kim attached.

When you see that, it is interesting. 

The best character is "Heaven" (天). Is that not the best character? When you look at the character "Heaven" (天), it represents two people. The character "Father" (父) is similar. What does "Father" (父) mean? It is connected to eight people. It is two groups of eight people combined. Isn't that so? This is the character for "person" (人). This indicates two people. Isn't that right? If you separate them, it means two people.

And the character "Husband" (夫) is interesting because this "Husband" (夫) has pierced through the heavens. It is indeed two people, but it is the character "Husband" (夫). Isn't that so? Therefore, the people who created Chinese characters in ancient times believed they received revelations through the heavens. Don't think that Mr. Moon's explanation is just impressive. (Laughter) This character "Husband" (夫) is said to be higher than heaven.

That is why God cannot be alone. It means He must have a partner. What does that mean? It means they must become a couple. When they become a couple, it becomes "Husband" (夫). Thus, it is said to be the highest. Isn't that right? Heaven is high, and the earth is the widest, but it is said to be higher than that. Everything consists of two people. Isn't that so? The character "Father" (父) also, if you remove this (八), it becomes a cross (十). Isn't that a cross? These two fathers become the restored fathers. (Laughter) It is interesting to see this. "Benevolent" (仁) and so on, these also all refer to two people, don't they?

From this perspective, what is good? Is being alone good? Would it be good to have just one eye here? If the ear is here and the tip of the head sticks out this much, it looks good. That is how it is. If my one eye becomes disabled, would it be good? Try to be that kind of person; is it good? Goodness cannot exist alone. That is why God is no exception.

God wants to visit a house that laughs and sings.
The other day when I went to Jeju Island, something unpleasant happened. When I go to Jeju Island, I usually buy a few pineapples as a souvenir. There used to be a place that sold pineapples a bit cheaper, but now it has moved about 8 kilometers away. I went to find that place. The owner lady was plump but had a pleasantly round face. It was like a white rice cake covered in black bean powder; it looked that way, but it tasted great and was very delicious... She was that kind of lady. I thought that since her face looked pleasant, she would surely have some money saved up by the next time I came.

Since I was in Jeju Island, I thought I would buy pineapples as a souvenir and went to that house, but I saw that they had created a large pineapple farm and built a Western-style house. Looking at the situation, it was a very well-organized house. I thought this was different from the house I had visited before, so I went in to meet the owner and buy pineapples, but I heard loud voices from the inner room, "Hey, you son of a gun! I didn't expect that from you!" It was quite impressive. With a voice mixed with half a dialect from Pyongan Province, "You son of a butcher!" (Laughter) and then, "I didn't expect that from you. Do you think you live in this house because you are so great? You must not forget me! It is because I am here that this is so!" Oh, the way that woman was weaving her words was impressive.

I thought for sure she was plump and had a round face, but seeing her again, it was indeed that same lady from before. When she saw me, she remembered me and said, "Oh, aren't you the person who came before?" "Is that so? I don't remember," I replied. If I said I remembered, it would be so embarrassing. (Laughter) It changes your attitude. So I said, "Oh, I once came to buy pineapples. I know you well." I greeted the lady. (Laughter) If I had just gone to buy pineapples, would I have felt good or bad? It felt strange.

"Hey, owner! Oh, where have you gone? Today is a spring day, and the weather is nice, so let's go to a sunny place and sing a song or dance! Is there a father so-and-so here?" If I had sung a song with a captivating melody, how nice would that have been? People like us are very emotional. So how nice would it be to dance lightly?

Would you want to visit a fighting house or a singing house? Which house would it be, a fighting house? "No." Do you like being praised in the Unification Church or being scolded? Which do you prefer? "Being praised." It is nice to be praised. However, even if the Unification Church's Teacher Moon gets scolded repeatedly, he takes it lightly. You feel bad when you get scolded, right? However, if something better comes after being scolded, then being scolded is also good. (Laughter)

From this perspective, would God want to visit a fighting house or a laughing and singing house? You all answer me. Which house would He visit? He visits the house that laughs and sings. When Teacher Moon of the Unification Church passes by somewhere, would he go to a house that prays, "Oh, I am hungry, please give me a bag of rice!"? Even if he is hungry, when he arrives, he would go to the house that prepares flour pancakes and a bowl of water, waiting for him. Which house would he go to? If I were God, or if you were the teacher, which house would you visit? Would you go to a house that says, "Oh, I am hungry, please bring me a bag of rice!"? No. Even if it is poor, he would go to the house that waits with sincerity, eating less. It is the same.

Become a person who can be welcomed.
"When I go to church today, since there was the 7.4 North-South Joint Declaration, the teacher will surely say something new this morning. Who knows, he might even stir things up." Those who thought this might feel good, thinking, "My prediction was right." But when it has nothing to do with them, it becomes meaningless. Even if you did not predict correctly, you must understand that the person who finds a place of value beyond the predicted value becomes the owner.

Do you understand? "Yes." When I tell you to go out to evangelize, what will you say? "Oh, I can't go because of my husband, I can't go because of my children!" Is that what you would say? Then when you die, can you avoid dying because of your children? Can you choose how you die? Can you freely live or die because of your children? As a believer, should you not live freely in life and death? Why can’t I live? The teacher is not that kind of person. Is the teacher of the Unification Church your servant?

Sometimes, while walking, I stop and ask myself, "Where are you going?" I am asking myself. "Where am I going? What am I going there for?" Then I wonder why I am going crazy. It should be a time to rest comfortably...

Yesterday, I came back from a place and it was past one o'clock at night. Today, I thought it was five o'clock and woke up, but it was three o'clock in the morning. When I go somewhere, I have to wake up an hour early to wash my face and pray. When I woke up, I had miscalculated the time. The teacher was in a hurry. The watch is a luminous watch, but I misread it. I thought the time was up and jumped up, saying, "Mom, the time is up, why aren't you getting up?" She said, "It's not even four o'clock yet, why are you saying that?" After that, can I go back to sleep because I woke up early? So I didn't sleep much. After finishing the story here, I have to go to Suwon around twelve to talk to the Japanese members, and then I have to go to Jongno Church. I don't even know where Jongno Church is. Is there anyone here who knows where Jongno Church is? If anyone knows, please answer. I guess Dongha knows.

The teacher wakes up early in the morning and does this work, and during the day, he has to go here and there, and in the evening, he has to go somewhere else. My life is so busy that I can't even catch my breath. I am tired. While I am doing this, those who are here at the headquarters are in a dream. Those people have no connection with the teacher. Such people will not be taken along in the future. When I say to follow, if they cannot follow... 

America and England must also be able to go together. It is like moving. Follow along, I say. They should make an effort to be welcomed in America, saying, "Oh, I will go to bring someone from Korea!" They should become people who can do that in the spirit world. So, they should be able to travel around the world, about 12 countries. How many people can follow like that? If there are people with a historical tradition who can be welcomed, even if I do not support them, they should automatically recognize that historical tradition and hold a welcome ceremony for them. Is there anyone like that? There is no way.

Looking at this, why are foreign members sitting here? Can they speak or understand? Yet, they come and sit here before you, while those who live in the homeland are all late. They come in later and sit... I feel embarrassed. It was good that the foreign members did not understand what was being said. Even if this is translated, certain things must be omitted from the translation. (Laughter)

It feels unpleasant, but there is nothing I can do about it. Isn't that right? Even piglets get licked by their mothers when something is on their eyes. No matter what, I must establish their position, somehow help them, and forgive them...

You must become the vanguard of North-South unification.
Looking at your eyes, it seems serious. You played well, but it is a disaster. Those who did not go this time... Did the association president go? "Yes." Where to?

Now is the time to stand on that land and say, "Heaven, what will you do with our country? If you loved this country, please save me!" We must unite with a heart that loves the country and rise above the North and South. With the absolute faith that our ancestors had in their unfortunate history, you must believe in God, believe in the teacher, and the teacher believes in you. The formation of the Religious Council did not come from anyone else. It was achieved through the Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. However, I am not someone who seeks power. Did you come here to seize power? You bastards! I hate such people the most. If there are such people among the heads of organizations in the future, they are our enemies!

Now is the time for thirty million people, husbands and wives divided between North and South, to become the heralds of peace in this country. If they go out like that, with the sound of liberation ringing, at the border of the 38th parallel, fathers and mothers or husbands and wives will embrace each other and shed tears of reunion, and as long as that 38th parallel becomes a line of gratitude before heaven, this Korea will achieve peaceful unification and be established as the kingdom of heaven. In that sense, we must recognize that the prayer period until this August is a serious period. Do you understand?

Break through the final barrier
From now on, we must criticize again. “Did you really love your country? Did you love the church? Did you love God? Did you love your teacher? Did you love God’s family?” We must criticize this again. The connections that heaven has provided through the connections of one’s own family on this earth, through tribes, nations, and the world, to establish the foundation of eternal welfare in heaven, if one breaks those connections into pieces and harbors a fragmented relationship while dreaming of today’s happiness, that person is doomed. They are doomed. Such a solemn time has come.

Those who are born with such a heart, live with such a heart, and die with such a heart will surely become citizens of the heavenly kingdom, become members of the heavenly family, and become sons and daughters of God.
