At the crossroads of good and evil
The church you belong to is Jongno Church. When you hear "Jongno," what impression comes to mind? You think of a bell. It is a street with a bell. There is a big bell in front of Hwashin, but it is not the Emile Bell; what kind of bell is it? Anyway, it reminds you of the Bell Tower.

We must ring the bell of good meaning
A bell is rung to announce new or special news to a wide audience. When the bell rings, we associate it with new events happening in the country, and we think that a special incident has occurred.

From this perspective, we Jongno Church members must always have a special mission to present new events in the Unification Church.

The person who has come here as the person in charge, Park Jong-gu, is someone with a strong pioneering spirit. He does not like to follow the path others take; he has a temperament that enjoys leading new endeavors that others have not done, which you have probably come to know over the past few months. As you all know, he had a significant influence when he established the Seonghwa Academy in Chungju on July 16, 1972. Therefore, I think it is because of the connection with Jongno Church that you have met such a leader.

In this sense, I hope Jongno Church can become a body that can create new events in the Unification Church and a church that presents new issues in Seoul.

So, what kind of bell should we ring to create a new sound, a new bell? We must ring a bell of good meaning. For the country, it should be a bell that announces good news to the entire population of Seoul, not a bell that announces bad news when the country faces misfortune.

There are two types of bell sounds. When we look at the events of a nation, we think there are two types of content for ringing a bell. One is good news, and the other is bad news. Thus, a bell is rung to announce the fate of the nation.

From this perspective, our Jongno Church members... Originally, I planned to tour the whole country this time, including Jongno and Seoul, but I could not do so. I could have created time for that, but since there were internal matters to organize and issues to resolve after the tour, I needed a special period, which is why it has been delayed until now, and I apologize for that.

However, Mr. Park came to me specifically the Sunday before and said, “You must come to Jongno Church on the 16th.” I did not make a definite promise to go, but I asked him to contact me again the day before. Today, I do not know if it is good luck or bad luck... This morning, the teacher spoke. Today, there are about 141 Japanese members at Sutaek-ri... They came yesterday. About 80 came by 2 PM yesterday, and the rest arrived at 11 PM, but I could not meet them... So, I made an appointment at 8:30 AM today, and that is why I am late.

Now, what I want to say before the members of Jongno Church today is that we must present an event. What kind of event should we present? We must present good events. In this context, the content of what I want to share with you today is “At the Crossroads of Good and Evil.” Let’s talk about this for a moment.

We can hope for good things, but it is not easy to attain good things
When we look at this world, there is no one from any country who does not think their own country is good. There is no country that does not think their own country is good. The same goes for nations, and when we look at our own families, there is no one who does not want to think their own family is good.

From this perspective, what about individuals? There is no individual who does not think well of themselves. Just as individuals, families, or nations want to boast about their own country being good, it is the true nature of humanity today.

However, while they love their own country, what about the world? When we look at this issue, there are not many who love the world. It is different. Therefore, when we look at humans until now, what they have wished for is to hope for their own well-being, for their own homes to be well, and for the country they live in to be well. This is what we know has been the goal pursued by humanity throughout history.
of the people of the Republic of Korea, when they go abroad, they immediately feel it. When they meet fellow Koreans in a foreign country, it is a joyful experience. Also, when a citizen of the Republic of Korea faces discrimination abroad, even though that person is unrelated to me, the frustration is indescribable. If I suffer sadness, I can endure it, but seeing a fellow countryman suffer sadness gives me an unbearable stimulus.

From this perspective, any people, any ethnicity, wishes for their country, their family, and themselves to be well. This has been the desire of humanity throughout history. However, you must understand that there are not many people who wish for the world to be well.

Moreover, in negative situations, the thought arises, "I must not be harmed. Even if others are harmed, I must not be harmed. Perhaps there may be bad things outside my home, but my family must not be harmed. And my country must not be harmed." This is the wish of people who have a nation, who have a family, and who respect themselves.

When wishing for good, people wish for good centered around themselves, and when wishing for bad, they wish for bad excluding themselves, their side, or their country. This is the desire of human beings. This is undeniable, isn't it? You all feel the same way. Everyone wishes for good things to be theirs and bad things to belong to others. However, when we analyze whether reality allows this to happen, we know all too well that it is not possible for me to only have good things and to only live in good places.

Some people strive for success and achievement, but such efforts are made by everyone. Even if there are millions of citizens, there is no one who does not wish for every individual among them to be well. Likewise, there is no one who wishes for a country not to be well. While everyone wishes for the whole to be well, the question arises whether many good outcomes actually appear, and the answer is no. Everyone wishes for good, but we often encounter worse outcomes than we hoped for.

If there were many good things, people would not speak of life as a sea of suffering or a fate of sorrow. Rather, because bad outcomes are more often associated with good outcomes, we come to say, "Life is sad. The path of life is like a sea of suffering." We must understand this. Therefore, while everyone wishes for good, we must recognize that it is not easy to possess good.

Establishing a clear standard for good
From this perspective, individuals must have a standard for wishing to be good. Families must have a standard for wishing to be good. Nations must have a standard for wishing to be good. If the standards differ between person A and person B, the fact that they wish for good becomes ridiculous. Therefore, when a thousand or ten thousand people say something is good, there must be content that everyone can agree on, stating, "This is good because of this." It is absurd to claim something is good without presenting such content.

Then, how should we define "good"? There must be a model or formula stating, "Individuals should be like this, families should be like this, and nations should be like this." Without such a framework, it cannot be done. That is the principle.

History does not develop centered around evil. When evil flourishes, history inevitably retreats. When good overcomes evil, history, or the historical environment, whether personal, familial, or national, advances. That is the principle.

So, what are the personal standards that can present good and evil? This is a critical issue. When we look at humanity, those who do not believe in God may think, "I can live according to my conscience. If I do not feel guilty, am I not justified?" But is everyone who has a conscience the same? They are not. Just as faces differ, the situations of their consciences also vary; some may be in higher positions, while others may be in lower positions. When we draw a line of good, and extend it horizontally from that vertical line, there will be people at 90 degrees, and others at 10, 20, or 30 degrees, representing a multitude of directions and positions.

Thus, the standard of being "conscientious" also becomes a problem.

From this perspective, while humans wish to be good, they live without clearly knowing how to achieve that goodness. Why should we be good? Why do we wish for good? How can we achieve goodness? In mathematical terms, one plus one equals two, and adding three makes five. Such resultant formulas are the same for anyone learning mathematics, transcending history and existing in any era. They can feel the same way. However, there has not been a clear standard or definition for good.

Then, where is the position of being "conscientious"? That is the question. Is it a higher position, a lower position? Is it beyond a certain boundary? Or, if it is internal, what position does it hold? When you look at yourselves, you are currently listening to the teacher. This is not a coincidence. It is a meeting through some predetermined connection.

Here, whether it is a young lady, a young man, or a student, there is a student named Roh Jeong-kyun. When called, he responds, "Yes!" If asked, "What did you do?" he will say, "I did this today." That incident is simple. If he fetched water, it concludes with the act of fetching water, but the historical connections leading to that moment stretch back millions of years.

The hand that fetched the water is Roh Jeong-kyun's hand, but it is not just his. Whose hand does it resemble? It resembles his father's and mother's hands. It does not only resemble his parents' hands; it also bears some resemblance to his grandfather's hands. Moreover, it is not just the grandfather but also the great-grandfather and many generations of ancestors. Thus, that hand represents the cells of thousands of ancestors. Therefore, when viewed from that hand, it is like the president of a hand corporation.

The same goes for the eyes. When looking at one eye, it blinks, and while it may seem like it is his eye, it is not just his. It is a product of accumulated connections, a condensed entity. If we examine the parts of that eye, the parts resembling the eyes of good ancestors will appear good, while parts derived from the cells of evil ancestors will appear bad. The eyes resembling good ancestors may not see bad things and will see good things clearly. It will be like that. When we observe this, we see how it is all integrated.

Nowadays, if we analyze a single hair, we can determine everything about a person's character and profession, just like a detective can analyze all the relationships behind that person and their environment. When we realize that we stand in a scientific age, we must understand that our parts, our limbs, are not solely ours. They are all interconnected.

The boundary between good and evil
From this perspective, the place where one feels good, saying, "Oh, this is good!" is it only good for that one individual? That place represents a peak of history. Therefore, it weighs history. When weighing, it should balance, but if it tilts a little, it goes this way, and if it tilts a little more, it goes that way. This boundary is uncertain, yet it can turn the world upside down. Such a boundary exists. A slight shift can lead to good, and a slight shift can lead to evil.

Thus, there must be a correct path. There must be an absolute standard that no one can infringe upon, which must not be added to even a little. There must be a degree to which individuals, families, nations, and the world can go. Isn't that so?

When we look at this, when asking who the type is that should be like this, can you say, "It is me!"? Have you thought about it? "Although I am a small girl, I stand at the center of a standard that encompasses all women in the world." Have you ever thought that way? If there were a scale that could measure with extreme precision, it would be able to determine whether something exists or not. Therefore, when looking at that central position, whether it exists or not becomes the issue. There must be something there.

When good and evil are in opposition, there will be a boundary. Right? When looking at the 38th parallel, where is that line? It passes through a buffer zone and draws a line. The 38th parallel is a thick line. The question of whether it exists or not is significant. From this perspective, if you ask, "Do you really know the 38th parallel?" the answer would be, "I know it." But if you probe deeper, you will find that they do not know what the 38th parallel is. It is a boundary that is both a boundary and not a boundary; it is a line that is both on one side and the other, yet not exclusively either side.

When it becomes morning and approaches lunchtime, can we definitively say it is lunchtime at twelve o'clock when the clock strikes? Just because the clock strikes twelve does not mean it is truly twelve o'clock. There is only one true time in the world. Wouldn't that be the case? We do not even know whether it has become twelve o'clock or not. This is a serious issue.

When spring comes and summer arrives, is there anyone who confidently says, "I know the boundary between spring and summer"? It just happens that spring arrives and summer comes without us even realizing it. Can we meet someone who knows when summer arrives? It is difficult to meet someone who truly knows.

Moreover, has anyone truly sent off spring while saying, "Ha ha! Spring, go now. Summer, come now"? Have you ever met such a person? Have you met them or not? "I have not met them." You have not met them, right?

When we think about it this way, is there truly good and evil? What is good? If good and evil exist, there must be a boundary. Good and evil create a boundary, and where good and evil intersect, there must be a crossing point. There must be a crossroads, a bifurcation point, but where is that? That is the question. Do you understand? The bifurcation point of good and evil is the issue. Do you understand?

Understanding the starting point of good
Today, we speak of "unification" and "the Unification Church," but where should unification begin? It should start from the foundation. Then, where does that foundation begin? "It starts from my home..." No, it does not. For a home to exist, there must be a father and a mother, and for a father and mother to exist, there must be a man and then a woman. Therefore, unification must begin with man and woman.

But is it enough to have just a man and a woman? It must go through a man whose body and mind are unified, and then through a woman whose body and mind are unified, to create a unified family. That is how it works, right?

If the body and mind are completely at odds, with the body wanting to go one way and the mind wanting to go another, can there be unification? Do your bodies and minds fight daily, or do they get along well? "They fight." They fight! Then, on which side do you stand? You stand on both sides. There are factions wanting to go where the body prefers and factions wanting to go where the mind prefers, so you have two factions within you.

Then, what kind of position is it where you can say, "Oh, I cannot live without you. You cannot live without me. So let us become one"? Have you figured that out? Have you figured it out or not? There must be a bifurcation point of good and evil within the individual.

Anyone who loves their mother, child, or wife more than me is not worthy. They must carry their own cross and follow me." Therefore, the Unification Church says to live according to the Bible. So, abandon your wife and step forward for the purpose; abandon your children and step forward for the purpose. What the established church does not know and what the pastors of the established church cannot do, the teacher of the Unification Church has done. He has stepped forward, abandoning his wife and parents. That is how he has lived. Yet, the one who lives that way is a heretic, and the one who cannot live that way is a true believer? There is no such heavenly principle!

World unification begins with me, who is united in body and mind.
Therefore, those who do not possess the standard of unity between body and mind, no matter how great their dreams or high their ideals, must understand that it is a principle that they cannot connect to the universal ties of the world. You, who stand at the crossroads of good and evil today, must be careful in your choices. Even when you wear clothes, do not take pleasure in receiving them as gifts. The people of the Republic of Korea will perish if they enjoy receiving handouts.

"Members of the Unification Church must live to give and live for others." Those who hold this belief will inevitably be determined by their center as time passes, so you must understand that even if you do not dream of success, success will automatically occur in your environment.

According to this principle, especially the youth must clearly understand that this is the standard of good and evil, and they must become tomorrow's victors, surpassing the shining liberation of the homeland to welcome a day of happiness when the world’s heavenly kingdom opens. Thus, I briefly spoke in hopes that you will not only receive God's love as princes and princesses of victory but also be recognized as those who can say to the nations to emulate this figure.

<Prayer> Loving Father! Please remember the young members of Jongno Church gathered here. Our gathering here is not by our own will. We have come together under the center of Heaven, following connections we may not even be aware of, so we must always remember that we stand in the position of the object before the subject.

I must understand that I exist for the sake of the object. I must recognize that when he is completed in pursuing values like mine, that completion returns to me. When I stand in such a position, I may lose one but can possess two, leading to a more valuable decision, which is good, and both can rejoice. This joy can become the center of happiness as it rises to a higher dimension, and through that center, Heaven can reaffirm the beginning of a new history, and I earnestly hope and wish that the young hearts here can make a new resolution.

Therefore, our Jongno Church is not fighting for Jongno Church alone but for Seoul and the Republic of Korea, so I sincerely hope that you will always be members who do not lose while keeping pace with the global humanity.

I thank you for allowing us to meet, and may the words spoken here become the lifeblood of these individuals. I earnestly ask that you allow us to be a stimulating group that admires you and can draw closer to you throughout our lives, and I pray all these things in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

5) Our Attitude
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is the fourth Sabbath morning of this month. May your infinite love, compassion, and mercy be with all your children across the nation as they look up to this place and worship before you.

We, the Unification group, are aware that we are in a critical time where we must gather our sincerity to fulfill the remaining mission of restoration. We hope for your special guidance and support during this special 40-day period of devotion.

Since humans are always insufficient, we realize how easily we can deviate from Heaven's desired will and standard. When we understand this, we feel once again how much we are subjects of concern in your arduous restoration path.

Father, do not leave us here alone at this time; please manifest yourself so that we can be children who are worthy of Heaven's expectations and love as we pledge for the final day and ultimate victory. Please watch over the small number of children gathered this morning. We know that humans are destined to follow your will. Moreover, as we consider that we are born as descendants of evil ancestors who have left behind countless sorrows in the restoration path, we cannot help but wish for your infinite love and protection to be added to us.

Father, please look down upon us at this time. We must have a longing for you in our hearts, stand by your side, and have a sincere desire to represent you. When we think of Heaven, we must not have habitual notions but should not let our days pass meaninglessly like the flowing time. Grant us the hearts that can pledge to walk the path of your will day by day.

Father! This July is now entering its latter half. As we reflect on this month in your holy will, we must consider what we have left before Heaven and what we have offered. We acknowledge that we are always in a position of insufficiency, so please allow us to be children who can fill that position with sincerity.

Father, while protecting your children across the nation, I hope you will also protect the world’s mobilization forces standing on the front lines according to this era's mission. Wherever they go, may you directly manifest yourself to reveal the authority of the living Father, and may all people be drawn to you through your guidance, allowing countless spirits in the spirit world to achieve a unified point through them, thus fulfilling the completion on earth and achieving the liberation of the spirit world.

When we think that all spirits that have come and gone cannot be completed without passing through us on earth, we must realize how significant our current position is. We have a vast mission that not only represents one era but also connects three eras, and we must recognize that our individual shortcomings can affect the past, present, and future. We must understand that through the completion of each individual, the past, present, and future can be offered to you in a new meaning, and we must realize how earnest we must be in fulfilling our duties of filial piety and loyalty before you.

Father! Please protect us at this time. Protect this day. May your abundant love never depart from every place where we pledge our loyalty according to your will, and may you be with those who are advancing before you, laying down their lives for your will, with your infinite power. I earnestly hope that the glory of victory will be with them.

Having stepped over the limits of restoration, may we serve you in victory, praise you, and, through you, be loved as members of one heavenly family, fulfilling our duties of loyalty and filial piety, and may we pledge to fulfill our responsibilities as the central beings of all nations. I earnestly hope and wish for this.

Please remember your children scattered across the world. Father, you must be especially with them wherever they are fighting on the front lines. In your manifestation, may your infinite power and authority personally support them from all sides, allowing them to have days of victory and presenting a new mission to all people while leaving nothing behind. I earnestly ask and wish for this. Please oversee everything. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Although the environments each of us faces may be limited, the environment of an individual can represent a family, that family can represent a society, that society can represent a nation, and that nation can represent the world.

An individual is not limited to just their own existence. When we think from this perspective, we realize that a single person is not limited to themselves. When we say "I," there is a family connected behind that "I," and that family is connected to the nation or the world.

From this viewpoint, we see that we simultaneously represent the world’s humanity, and if Heaven stands in a subjective position regarding this land, then our individual existence not only represents the earth but also stands in place of the subject, Heaven. Therefore, the attitude of one person is not formed and concluded in isolation; it connects and extends beyond society, nation, and the world.

Thus, when we trace historical events, we find that once a historical event becomes a historical standard, it can be remembered as something significant, yet at the time, many such events were not widely recognized or treated as important. We understand that even the most significant historical events were not always accepted as such by society or the nation at the time.

Moreover, after time passes, we come to recognize certain individuals or events as historical events in the next era. 

From this perspective, when we look at the life of Jesus Christ, we see that during his thirty years of life, everything he did was not recognized as valid at that time. The environment he faced was not one that supported him but one that opposed him. The Judaism of that time, the Israelite people, had the Messiah they longed for, yet there were very few who could recognize him as the Messiah. This fact is undeniably tragic from a human perspective. For Judaism, it was a cold and painful moment that could foretell its decline.

God nurtured the nation of Israel over four thousand years as a chosen people, leaving behind a thread of hope because the Israelite people were to send the Messiah. However, despite the fact that the environment was set for each individual of the Israelite nation to connect with the hope of the Messiah, they failed to become a nation that welcomed that existence.

Thus, after sending the one who came, the nation and the denomination that chased him away without understanding his will faced dire consequences, as we know from history. However, God, who sent him, knew very well what mission he had on earth and what responsibilities he needed to fulfill. Therefore, regardless of whether society welcomed him or the era accepted him, God overcame the negative environment and pioneered a positive one. We know that Christianity has inherited that mission and developed according to that will. 

After history has passed, we come to know what mission he came with and remember and commemorate him.

Humans who do not know the heavenly fortune
When we see this, we realize that people do not know when or how their life's fate will unfold. Just as one does not know the exact moment when morning crosses into noon, or when midnight connects morning and evening, we often do not know when these transitions occur. Although we have the concept of time and a clock to tell us the hour, that specific time is neither before nor after; it is a line that may seem nonexistent.

In our lives, we may easily overlook when opportunities for success or failure will come and how they will relate to us.

Just as this is true for individuals, it is also easy to forget when and how the fate of a nation will arrive and pass. We must recognize that if we understand this appropriately and align our intentions with the beginning, we can determine how the end should be.

In this way, the fate of the world is the same. We do not know when misfortune will come to this world or when it will align with Heaven's will to achieve a time of victory. Even if that time comes, we know from historical facts and our daily lives that it is difficult to accept it directly.

Therefore, those who bear great missions or responsibilities must always be vigilant and aware of their path. There are many situations where they must remain alert and focused. If a leader makes a mistake, the entire group associated with them may face misfortune. Even if that leader suffers in a position of misfortune, if they resolve it in alignment with heavenly fortune, what may seem miserable at the time can become a sacred moment of historical victory in retrospect.

The more we think about this, the more we must realize that an individual's life is not solely their own. Even those who bear important responsibilities do not act alone; those who follow the decisions made by such individuals are not alone either. Although they may act independently, there is always a historical connection. This connection comes from their ancestors; if their ancestors were good, they follow the lineage of good, and if they were evil, they follow the lineage of evil, resulting in the outcomes they experience. Their paths are inevitably influenced by these connections. At this moment, how one decides and resolves can lead to the acceptance of a new era or the rejection of it.

How to respond to victory or despair
From this perspective, what should our attitude be as members of the Unification Church standing in the present situation? We must never be self-satisfied. We humans cannot afford to be self-satisfied. The moment we boast of a victory we have achieved can become the final announcement of joy in our lives, and at the same time, it may lead to even greater misfortune because of that end. One can boast of a scene, and as soon as that boast ends, greater sorrow may follow. Moreover, in some respects, one may be surrounded by misfortune...
In a place of deep despair, one might say, "I am now despair itself. I cannot go any further. I cannot hope for anything beyond this." However, through some connection with someone, it is possible to rise from despair with new hope and new aspirations. 

When we see it this way, we realize that a person can never fully possess themselves, and while they may grieve, they cannot simply mourn in a state of despair. If there is something to boast about, that boast should not end with today’s pride. If there is something to be proud of, it should become a shining legacy for tomorrow. A boast that ends with today is not acceptable. If it becomes just a boast of today, then when misfortune comes next, that misfortune will be even more tragic, and one might feel that it would have been better not to have boasted at all.

Therefore, even if there is joy, we should hope that the joy connects to a more brilliant purpose. Standing in a joyful place with the heart that desires to connect that joy to a higher victory tomorrow, we must pledge to have a secondary or higher aspiration that humbly looks forward. If one stands in such a place, after the pride in their joy has ended, no matter how much misfortune approaches, they will possess the strength to break through that misfortune.

No matter how much despair one is in, that despair does not have to end in despair. The affairs of the world operate according to principle. If there is a time of elevation, there will also be a time of decline. We know that the sunny and shady sides alternate.

When we think this way, we realize that no matter how sad a situation one stands in, that sadness must come to illuminate a joy that can shine even brighter. When we digest that sadness and welcome it as joy, if joy comes afterward, that joy will indeed shine even brighter than the depth of that sadness. From this perspective, we must understand that no matter how sad things may be, those who have the strength to overcome that time for the brilliant joy that can come afterward will not end there.

The Israeli people had to wait with a heart of patience
From this perspective, when we look at the Israeli people who welcomed Jesus, we see that Jesus, being sent from heaven, is the most precious figure among the Israeli people when viewed from heaven. The appearance of Jesus in the historical process of the Israeli people is one of the greatest historical events. This is the maximum joy that could be before the Israeli people, yet we know that his appearance did not come with content that could bring joy.

When viewed in light of all the truths that they boasted about and regarded as the foundation of their happiness in the Old Testament era, these all appeared in a conflicting and destructive form. Therefore, the Israeli people and Judaism tried to confront this directly to resolve it, and we must recognize that there were mistakes on the part of the Israeli people and failures on the part of Judaism.

When we look at Jesus, we see that he is not an ordinary person. His actions were remarkable throughout history. He could be looked up to from all directions, and the environment could be moved… However, we must understand that when his position was encroached upon and he was pushed aside, it led to a great failure in how they treated Jesus.

If they had not stood in such a position and had approached Jesus with the mindset that "his appearance is meant to give us some advice and to pass on something new to us," and if they had waited with the unique national strength that no one else possessed, the strength that had upheld heaven's will for 4,000 years, they would not have become a tragic nation suffering from historical disasters.

If, in such a position, they had reassessed Jesus and judged that the outcome would be good, and had aligned with him, the Israeli people would not have become such a tragic nation in history. This is something we can understand when we look back at history.

For Jesus' disciples, his death was extremely tragic. For Peter and the twelve disciples, the death of Jesus was akin to the severing of their lifeline. All their values were eradicated from that point. However, if those disciples had not been hasty, but instead had centered on the words Jesus spoke, which taught that despair does not end in despair, and if they had gone forth with patience, Peter and the twelve apostles would not have stood in a position where they failed to recognize God.

Before Jesus, the Israeli people indeed became a tragic nation, but the disciples, who inflicted an unspeakable blow on him as he approached death, were the ones who suffered the most. When a servant came out during the trial and asked Peter, "Aren't you also a Galilean?" Peter denied it without hesitation. If he had held the belief that "standing in such a trial does not mean the end of history; rather, a new history starts from here," and had focused on the past based on that belief, standing firm while envisioning new hope, he would not have left a tragic mark in history.

To overcome immediate problems or environments
Looking at this, we can see that many members of the Unification Church believe in the church because they have their own motivations. When Unification Church members go out to evangelize, whether it be through women or men, they come in contact with the teachings. Of course, the words are spoken by the Unification Church evangelists, but those words are not only heard by them. They receive those words as higher teachings. After hearing, they feel their hearts being drawn. Many people unknowingly decide to become members of the Unification Church. We know that the spiritual world is directly involved behind this.

We are well aware of the facts that heaven participates in guiding us to establish our lives on this path. If I were to deny this path, we must understand how much effort heaven puts forth to defend it in various ways. Among the members of the Unification Church who have gone through such a history, when they encounter difficulties on their path, we often see people who fall away midway, become discouraged, or tire out, simply treating those difficulties as mere hardships.

Not all matters begin with good things. Try eating only sweets every day; there is nothing more painful than that. To truly understand the stimulating aspect of sweetness, one must taste bitterness. After tasting bitterness, one can experience a sweeter and brighter sweetness.

Even when we look at the waves transmitted through the air, they are transmitted through a relationship of density and sparsity. They do not travel in a straight line all at once. Everything has its time; one time follows another. When that connection occurs, there are boundaries. The present time is not the same as the time that will come next, and to connect them, there must be something that is not normal, something different from the current normal environment, through which new events can be connected.

Having entered the Unification Church and recognized that they are being guided by heaven, we see many who are swayed by changes in their environment. No matter what changes occur, if one can break through that environment in a straight line, that change can broaden the foundation for tomorrow's hopes and solidify tomorrow's traditional foundation. However, we must recognize how often our own agitation has led to the destruction of the new foundation of blessings that are to come.

Therefore, when faced with any problem, we must be able to discern between right and wrong. If there are good things today, we must recognize that there may be sad things that follow behind them, and that sadness and good things are relative.

The normal process for bearing fruit
When a seed is sown, it must go through several stages to bear fruit. A sprout must emerge, then a stem, then branches, then leaves, and flowers must bloom before fruit can be produced. The emergence of the cotyledon and the stem is different. The branching from the stem is also different. The emergence of leaves from branches is different. The blooming of flowers from leaves is yet another difference. The bearing of fruit from flowers is also different. However, the whole process is one event.

If one stands in denial of the differences that arise from the cotyledon to the stem, they will not be able to produce branches. If one denies the branching from the stem, they will not see the leaves. If one denies the emergence of leaves from branches, they will not see the flowers. Those who deny the emergence of leaves and the blooming of flowers will not see the fruit. This is one event. This is the inevitable path of fate to complete a task. The new sprout must emerge from the seed. It must emerge no matter how mismatched it may seem. The stem must extend branches sideways. It cannot just go straight up; branches must emerge. Leaves must emerge from the branches. And flowers must bloom. There must be a fruit borne from that flower. This is the normal process.

Considering that a tree goes through this process from sprout to fruit, we must recognize that as a human being moves toward perfection, or as a nation seeks completion, or as the world moves toward a time of completion centered on God's providence, if one only hopes for good times, this is abnormal.

As you learned in the Principle, there are stages of restoration, growth, and completion in the period of restoration, and the same applies to the growth period and the completion period. When we look at the whole, the stages of restoration, growth, and completion refer to a transformative form. We must understand that we can hope for a developmental outcome that can absorb the environment harmoniously without conflict.

When we see it this way, as members of the Unification Church today, each of you is different. Just as each face is different… The fact that each face is different indicates that each person is a descendant of ancestors who have walked different historical paths. Thus, I was born. The "I" is not just a singular entity. It is the product of historical ancestors. And that product does not end with me. It continues. Today's "I" is determined as a future ancestor.

Then, in terms of a tree, how much a leaf stands in a fulfilling position to absorb nutrients and contribute to the growth of the entire tree can determine the direction of the branches.

Do not jump to conclusions about any problem; remain calm
When we see it this way, we must recognize that the position we are currently in is the most serious one. If we are not careful, we may ruin the past, but if we are careful, we can illuminate the past.

What is good today cannot guarantee that it will be good tomorrow. What is good today could also become the basis for sorrow tomorrow. Similarly, what is sad today does not end with today's sorrow. It can also present a good opportunity to inherit a foundation for tomorrow's goodness.

When we think this way, we must remain calm when facing any historical facts or real environments. We must not jump to conclusions. We must endure and reflect on it for a long time.

Even if a random event passes by me, if I continue to resolve it, could it not create some connection for me? Those who think about such problems repeatedly and resolve them are wise.

Many people often regret their decisions. "Ah, I wish I hadn't done that…" Such regrets arise. If one reflects deeply on such issues and decides, "This is a pledge regarding myself and my life," then they must take responsibility for it. Regret should not exist.

If one knows their own character and values what they have decided, then even if that decision leads to failure, if they can accept that failure graciously, such a person is needed. However, those who cannot take responsibility for their failures and make excuses are not welcomed in the human world. If humans do not welcome them, history will welcome them even less, and if history does not welcome them, God will welcome them even less.

The true attitude toward joy and sorrow
Therefore, for us who possess such an environment, the most important thing is the attitude we must take. So how should we take that attitude? When there is joy, do not respond only with joy. This is wisdom. Just because there is joy does not mean we can only take a one-way street with it. When there is joy, do not respond only with joy. If that joy can become a motive for sorrow because of me, we must accept it calmly. We must analyze it. If we do not accept that joy as our own but see it as belonging to a third party, and then, after testing it, share it as our own… Those who make such a commitment and accept it as their own to manage and digest it can develop.

If there is sorrow, the same applies. Do not accept sorrow as your own; rather, accept that sorrow as belonging to a third party, and if you can completely digest it as your own, that sorrow cannot ruin you. On the contrary, what was once sorrowful can become a new hope and a good chance to gain trust from the surrounding environment. "That person had such sorrow, yet despite that sorrow, they…"
"Ah, so it's being digested and passed on." When that happens, that personality is indeed a good condition to be trusted as a central being capable of taking responsibility for problems beyond the surrounding environment. It may be a loss for oneself, but it can be said to be a result that can benefit the environment.

We need such an attitude in these matters... especially in our faith life. Just because we saw something, we shouldn't jump to conclusions saying, "I saw it with my own eyes..." We shouldn't make hasty judgments just because we heard something. If we observe and relate it to ourselves with the thought, "I need to develop. I need to advance further," the question is how we can digest that in the direction of our advancement. How do we digest it? How do we accept it? Here, sadness is not necessarily all bad, and joy is not necessarily all good. Depending on how we digest it, sadness can sometimes be better than joy, and you need to understand this.

Therefore, isn't such an attitude necessary for a believer? This is not just an attitude that believers should have. It is even more necessary for those who carry responsibility. When a responsible person receives a report from someone, they should not make hasty judgments but rather discern it, weighing the results before and after, and when the outcome might affect the entire environment, they need to defend against it. They should also know how to withhold it if it can benefit the overall environment. If they forget that and just move on, thinking it can benefit the whole, they should be able to do that as well. You need to understand that a person who makes hasty judgments about everything related to themselves cannot be responsible for significant matters.

How did God respond to the fall of Adam and Eve? 

If we think about it centered on God, what kind of being is God? What is God's relationship with humanity? "Humanity has fallen." This is a drastically transformative event. It is an extremely problematic event that should not have happened. Faced with this event, God had the issue of immediately punishing the fallen humans... But when He expelled them from the Garden of Eden, did God immediately say, "You guys!" and cast them out? What do you think? Would He have expelled them immediately after the fall? He did not do that. He allowed Adam and Eve to understand what their "fall" meant before casting them out. A judge in a court, when determining a criminal, should tell the criminal, "You have committed such and such a crime, and therefore you must face such and such consequences." This is what a fair judge does.

When we look at it this way, did God immediately punish the fallen Adam and Eve? If they did not know about it, wouldn’t He have given them time to deeply understand it? He did not punish them immediately out of sadness; rather, they needed to feel responsible for the consequences before being punished. Of course, that would have been the case. So it was not immediate; there was a temporal distance. Because of the pangs of conscience, rather than being expelled immediately, Adam and Eve, feeling increasingly guilty, would have prayed to meet God again, wouldn’t they? Isn’t that the case in the world? Thus, knowing that they could not bear the weight of their sin, Adam and Eve would have thought, "It would be better not to show my face before God," and God waited until that thought arose before casting them out.

Therefore, Adam and Eve, being expelled, must have shed tears as they left. They would have lamented their decision to abandon such a compassionate and loving parent, God, rather than blaming heaven and shedding tears in anger. It is likely that they stood in the position of being expelled after a long period of time. 

In the spirit world, it is the same. When one goes to the spirit world, it is not that God sends them to heaven, nor is it that someone sends them to hell. They decide for themselves.

Now, think about how much God must have suffered during that period. He stood in a position where tragedy and comedy intersected, but because He was in a position to overcome it, a heart of compassion to save humanity must have arisen. The very act of overcoming and enduring, though it was painful and frustrating, must have led to finding a key to open the door of salvation.

When we think about these issues, we can see that God dealt with the situation from that perspective, and we too are not different. God must have stood in a place of deep sorrow regarding the expelled Adam and Eve. Originally, they should not have been in such a state... Isn't that the case in the world? A truly loving child, when they had not sinned in the past, could naturally come to their parents and be embraced without any wrinkles of shame on their face. However, when they do something wrong and act timidly, not naturally, the parents suffer in that environment, don’t they? In that case, doesn’t the parent's heart want to make it natural again? When something unnatural becomes significant, sympathy naturally arises.

Therefore, when conflicting circumstances confront us, those who try to resolve everything with that alone are all one-sided people. 

When faced with sadness, what should we do? 

From this perspective, what should be the attitude of a believer, our attitude? When I find myself in a position where I can shed tears, for whom should those tears be shed? We need to consider the origin of those tears. If the tears are shed only for myself, then they should not affect a third party. You need to understand this. Some people, when they experience sadness, stir up the environment and create a mess, making others sad because they are sad, thinking that will ease their own hearts. That is wrong.

Whose sadness is it? If it is sadness caused by a purpose, then everyone should know how to be sad together, and it is justifiable to express that sadness as the sadness of the whole. However, if it is sadness caused by oneself, then one must never impose that on the purpose or the whole. One must be the kind of person who resolves their own issues. If there are such people, God would want to entrust them with even greater responsibilities. If God exists, such a person is destined to be elevated to a higher position than where they currently stand. This is the same in human affairs.

For this reason, from this perspective, our attitude as believers... the path of faith is not something that is traveled in a day. It is not something you believe today and abandon tomorrow. It extends beyond a lifetime into eternity. Even in the spirit world, we must believe in God. We must carry God with us. We must believe in a higher meaning. 

In our faith life, there must be an unchanging core. 

Humans do not always live being loved. In the midst of conflicting situations in various fields, as the types of work differ, when one is placed in a position to work, God does not command with love. He pursues whether you did your work well or poorly. That does not mean love is absent. Because the stance is different, centered around work, one cannot develop or reach a higher position, and if one cannot reach a higher position, they cannot establish a higher connection of love. Thus, in this perspective, can we not digest all the challenges we face into happiness? This attitude is the most precious, and we must consider this.

Believing in God is not something done overnight. It is a lifelong endeavor. In the midst of our faith life, even if I die, I must maintain my faith centered on eternity. I must uphold that principle. You need to understand this clearly. There must be a central core. Because it is a path that must be believed in forever, one must discover that they cannot deny it. Do you understand what I mean?

If one is born as a child of their parents, there must be a principle that says, "I cannot be unfilial to my parents, even if it means death." Only then can they be a child who is always trusted by their parents. A person without such determination can become unfilial at any moment. Similarly, in our faith life, there must be an unchanging core. There must be a core. What is it? "No matter what difficulties I face, even if my own sadness lasts forever, I cannot present my own suffering as God's suffering. I cannot deny that I came out to serve the Heavenly Parent. I cannot establish a principle of denial against heaven." This principle must be upheld. That is the most precious thing. Most people cannot do this. A person who thinks, "I exist and God exists, the filial son exists and I exist, the loyal subject exists and I exist," is neither a filial son nor a loyal subject.

One must not become a barrier to eternity. 

The path of faith is not a path taken in a day. Because it is an eternal path, one must not become a person who sullies eternity. You must understand this. Among those who believe in God, there are many who block the eternal path with issues they cannot take responsibility for. Look at Judas Iscariot in the historical era. At that time, Jesus said, "I wish I had not been born," indicating that he was wrong. He judged based on his temporary desires, despite the path of eternal life he should have been following. This is an extremely reckless act. But can one avoid that path? After a few days, if they try to return to their old ways, no matter how hard they try, once they commit such acts, there is no way back. That is what leads to their doom.

Based on a single mainstream standard, even if it means I die or collapse, I must not speak a decisive word. You need to understand this. 

When you observe Unification Church members, there are many who are like weeds. If they know that this is the path they must take, they should not speak ill of the teachers leading that path or of God. Such people are like mayflies. They must understand that what they say can cut their own throat and bind their entire being. Once they speak, they must take responsibility for those words. That responsibility must be borne throughout their life, and if they cannot fulfill that responsibility, it will affect their descendants as well. Therefore, God does not keep such people close. Do you understand what I mean?

The path of faith in the Unification Church is a path one walks with their life. Therefore, it is not about making judgments about the path of mainstream action. It is extremely serious.
