May you govern the whole and lead the future of the Republic of Korea with these people, protect this Asia with them, and I earnestly ask you to safeguard the world. I hope that your love will be with all movements during this period, and I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We know that this created world is one object of God. We understand that God created all things for the fulfillment of His wishes.

The highest purpose of God in creating the created world
Happiness, satisfaction, or joy cannot be achieved alone. No matter how omnipotent He is, He cannot feel happiness or satisfaction alone, nor can He feel joy. Joy and happiness are established only in relative relationships. In other words, happiness can only be pursued in a place of giving and receiving.

In this regard, God is no different. If He rejoices alone as the Absolute, that is not normal. Just as we see in human life, God must have a relative standard to feel the stimulation of joy. If I give to Him, He must also return to me; in other words, all relationships and connections are established in the act of giving and receiving. Relationships are formed through connections, and through those relationships, unique progress is made, whereupon people feel satisfaction and gain new hope.

From this perspective, the created world that God has made exists for God's love. What is the highest ideal? Of course, there are things to see and enjoy, and things to want to live with, but what is the highest purpose? It is to center on love. To see is to see through love, and to live is to live centered on love. We understand that all things were created to establish connections through the stimulation and satisfaction of love.

Human beings are the absolute object that can receive God's infinite love.
From this viewpoint, we can see that among all things, the most precious is humanity. Among all things created by God, the masterpiece is human beings. We know that such humans are created as God's children.

If there is a God who is the subject of love, there must be an object that can receive that subjective love. We understand that there cannot be another being besides humans as that object. Therefore, we must become the ones who are qualified to receive God's absolute love. Just as there must be a vessel that can hold a certain amount of water to contain that amount, if God has infinite love, there must be a counterpart that can receive that infinite love. Thus, humans, created in a relative position before God, who has absolute love, cannot be seen as anything less than those who are in a position to receive and have more than enough of that absolute love.

Therefore, when God's infinite and supreme love comes upon us humans, it is not that God created humans to stand in a position of giving and receiving in a contradictory and conflicting place. We must be relative beings who can infinitely receive that deep love and also infinitely return it, so that God can be pleased. Furthermore, when we humans stand in a relative position to God, who is the subject of such love, we finally feel infinite love.

A happy place cannot be achieved by one person rejoicing alone. Both must rejoice. Moreover, when the environment involved and related to them is also captured by the environment of joy, the whole becomes a happy environment. Such a happy environment can become an ideal world where the entire created world, centered on humanity, is unified. In that case, whether high or low, we can understand that they will ultimately be in the same relationship of love.

When we look at the sun, the counterpart receiving sunlight is bright, and we come to know that the position of the bright world is undoubtedly a world centered on God's love. Such a world is the earthly paradise that God desired, and we think that the heavenly paradise connects this paradise.

We have five senses. Those senses are not only related to ourselves. Through all the sensory organs we possess, a higher dimension of God's love dwells. Therefore, we must establish relationships through those five senses, both in horizontal and vertical aspects.

In this light, our entire existence, living centered on those five senses, is not created merely to relate to ourselves but to relate to the subject, God. This is an undeniable fact. Therefore, we cannot deny that all intuitions or perceptions that our entire being feels are not centered on ourselves but are connected to the relative ideals, establishing internal connections that allow us to exist in a way that we can all be happy.

In the relationship between subject and object, the issue always at stake is that if there is giving, there must also be returning. If it becomes one-sided, the relationship cannot continue. It must be a process of giving and receiving. In giving and receiving, the broader and thicker it is, the more it becomes a standard for measuring happiness. Thus, the longer the time spent in giving and receiving well, the more it contains the content of elevating dimensions.

In our human relationships, as we get to know each other, the longer that period lasts, the more we can connect on a practical level. Not only that, but emotional issues also become intertwined. My living position and the comprehensive field I occupy want to establish a unified place with the counterpart I relate to. The larger, broader, and higher it is, the more that person will be an indispensable friend or family member before me. The longer that period lasts, it does not lead to bad outcomes but rather results in good outcomes. This is the nature of human relationships, where we wish to connect and expand infinitely to reach the realm of infinite happiness.

Thus, when something good happens to oneself, no one wishes for it to be temporarily good. We wish for good things to last forever. Furthermore, when a family does well, it is not just a temporary wish for them to do well; we wish for them to do well forever. If the parents do well, the children also wish to do well, and so do the descendants.

In this way, that connection becomes a nation. When viewed from the perspective of that nation, one wishes for the country they live in to be a happy nation. They hope that happiness is not temporary but lasts forever. We can infer that this connection extends to the world, not only to the tangible world but also to the intangible world, the eternal world. Therefore, my joy must not be my joy alone but must be a joy that can be shared with others.

Heavenly fortune is bound to support relative connections.
Therefore, in the realm of existence, there is nothing that does not have relative connections. That is how it is. Thus, if there is heavenly fortune, that heavenly fortune is bound to support relative connections. This is the principle of the world of existence. It is like a formula. Therefore, if it does not conform to that formula, the cosmic opposing force corresponding to that weight will act. If one has a counterpart worthy of heat, then heavenly fortune will support that heat. It is from there that all relationships are intended to operate through that center. We understand that this is the principle of the relative world of existence.

When there is opposition to that principle or when a defect arises, heavenly fortune will drive it away from the opposing position by that amount. For example, when a man and a woman become one centered on love, that is seen as a true couple. It is viewed as an ideal couple. Also, in the parent-child relationship, when the parents love their children wholeheartedly and the children who receive that love become the objects of joy, that parent-child relationship is seen as an ideal relationship.

In this way, when we look at the relationship between a man and a woman centered on love, when they stand in a position where they can give and receive God's complete love, they can finally become a couple who are objects of joy before God. When they completely give and receive centered on love, they become an ideal couple. At that time, the cosmic power protects and supports them, but when that love is lacking, it will inevitably drive them away by the amount that is lacking.

When people who love each other live together and one of them dies, why is there sadness? Why does one feel heartache and pain that is unbearable? It is not that one feels pain because they want to feel it. It is felt naturally. Even without having any sad motives or factors in their hearts, or longing or pursuing any stimulating desires, it is felt naturally. Why does it feel that way? It is because the principle of the universe supports the oneness of complete love.

When one deviates from this, it is driven away by a reaction. In other words, they become disqualified from the universal law. Disqualified individuals cannot exist in the same position within the realm of universal law. Therefore, naturally, to uphold that principle, it drives away through opposing actions. Thus, it can establish a perfect ideal standard. From this perspective, sadness is felt when the power of the universe acts upon me.
Love is realized in the position of caring for the other.
This is the same in the relationship between a father and son. When children and parents completely give and receive love, and when couples also give and receive love centered around that love, that is where ideals are realized. When we look at it this way, the existence of a man is not for himself but for a woman. Likewise, a woman exists for a man. If a man exists only for himself, that is a problem. We must understand that he was not born for himself.

In loving a child, parents do not love from a position that asserts, "Parents should be this way," with some fixed form. Rather, they love from a position that does not assert themselves, that denies themselves, in other words, from a place where they are not present. In other words, parents do not love their children from a position of authority but love them from a place that forgets their authority, even from a higher position. Is that not what it means to be a parent who approaches their child with such love?

The love that exists in parents is not for themselves but for the children. This love, which is called parental love, is not only for the parents but is for their counterpart. The same goes for children. When a child loves their parents, that love is not for the child but for the parents. Ultimately, the word love does not establish itself centered around oneself but is established in respecting the other more than oneself. Therefore, the very idea that one was born for love is connected to being born for the other.

The ideal unity is to become one centered around love.
Then, when we look at the pursuit of such an ideal love, if I was born for love, then I must exist for love. Being born is not the purpose; it is to love that one is born. What this means is that one must exist to fulfill a relative ideal, not to complete a subjective existence.

From this perspective, the question is whether we humans have ever fully received God's love centered around such an ideal of creation. God is omniscient and omnipotent, and at the same time, He is the Absolute Being. When we seek the authority and attributes that the Absolute Being possesses, has He ever fully given all His absolute authority, absolute value, and absolute love that pursues the object to humanity? This is the issue. If He had, then in a place where love is fully given and received, we would become completely one. It would not be two but one.

When we say "human," we refer to both men and women. It is when these men and women become one that they become human. To become one does not mean to become one based on form. It does not mean that the forms of men and women become mixed up, resulting in someone who is neither a man nor a woman. To become one means to unite centered around ideals. The term "one body of husband and wife" refers to this ideal.

So what is that ideal? It is happiness! What is happiness? It is the path of joy! In this light, the realization of that ideal is found in love. Therefore, to become one means to be unified centered around love, not centered around the counterpart.

Often, when discussing principles, we mention the unity of God's ideals. What does the unity of ideals mean? It does not refer to men and women with different faces. It does not refer to beauty or lack thereof. The unity of ideals refers to being united around love that has no higher ideal. That is an undeniable fact.

When the reality of God's ideal love appears,
From this perspective, when the absolute God faces relative humans in a position where He can be completely joyful, has He ever loved us, who are His unique counterparts? If humanity had not fallen, there would have been people who were loved based on this principle.

The fall refers to a loss. It speaks of incompleteness. It does not refer to a lack of something. It does not refer to a place where something is missing, but rather to a place where an ideal completion has not been achieved based on normal standards.

From this standpoint, if there exists a perfect God, when He sees something imperfect, can He have the heart that says, "Oh! I want to love"? When a creator makes a work, if what the creator envisioned is 100 percent perfect, but what is desired only turns out to be 90 percent, then there remains a 10 percent regret. Only by adding that can one stand in a position of complete happiness, where one can truly say, "Oh, I am so happy!" Therefore, if one has achieved 90 percent completion, one can love at the level of 90 percent, but cannot love at the level of 100 percent. When viewed this way, the same applies even to 99 percent. Wouldn't one then hope to love at 100 percent?

In the highest position, centered around human completion, is there an object that can be loved in a position where the perfect subject says there is nothing beyond this? One must meet such a person as a subject. When we think about this, a world that acknowledges the fall cannot exist.

Originally, God had the desire to love, but when He looks at an environment where that desire cannot be fulfilled, He is not a God of joy. If He wishes for 100 and only gets 90, He cannot be happy. You must have thought this when you were in school: "When I take the exam, I will surely get 100. I swear I will get 100. This is my ideal." After studying hard, if you did not get 100 but got 99 or 99.999, can you boast about that? It is at the same level as 100, but can you raise your hand and boast about it? The more absolute one is, the more absolute it must be.

From this perspective, when God looks at us humans, who are the ideal counterparts, and truly enjoys us, with a beaming smile, forgetting Himself, can He say, "This place, this path is my happiness. The creation of heaven and earth shines because of this person. I feel good"? Has there ever been such an ideal human? Could God have loved humanity in that way? He could not. Why? Because humanity has fallen. That is an undeniable fact.

Then, how beautiful would the original human form that could receive such love from God have been? When we look at it, would it not have been a symbol of beauty that could surpass the highest peaks expressed by world-renowned poets, capable of loving as a symbol of beauty? Would it not be so?

When the inner memory of oneself appears as reality, and when all the longing of one's inner self can manifest as an attractive beauty, how much would God have praised that appearance? Even the smallest thing could be a symbol of His love and an object of His joy. Is that not true? We know that gifts exchanged between lovers become unforgettable mementos throughout their lives. Even a handkerchief cannot be exchanged for a fortune.

When lovers look into each other's eyes, they express their love and joy, swearing on the entirety of their creative ideals. Would it not be endless? Whether looking at the nose, ears, face, back, or front, every part of the body, even to the fingertips, would not it be pleasing? He is undoubtedly a being who can praise centered around God's love. Within that realm of love, when one is immersed in that love, can one not testify, "This is how happy it is"?

Is there any unhappiness for a person standing in such a position? If God looks at His hands and rejoices, then I can feel that joy, so those hands must be beautiful hands. Moreover, when I look at my own reflection in the mirror, my body reflected in the mirror is completely taken by God, appearing as a 100 percent qualified product before God, stimulating God's love, and being a hopeful being that can stimulate eternally. When I think of that, how satisfied would I be to see such a self? Wouldn't that be possible? Isn't that true? When a husband loves his wife, and the wife sees that face and feels, "This is the face of my loving husband," the dignity of that face and the value of that beauty are multiplied.

When viewed this way, how ideal would it be if the reality of God's ideal love appeared after the creation of this universe? Today, while humans praise love in psalms and songs of songs, how wonderful would it have been if God, with all His joyful heart, sang songs like the psalms and left records of love like the songs of songs? Would that not have become the standard of love for humanity, the tradition of emotional life where love moves, and history? Would humanity today be unhappy?

The stimulation of God's love is eternal.
From this perspective, the "world governed by heaven" is not a world that exercises power just because it has some authority or omnipotent ability. Power can act as a force that supports and pushes love to be stronger, brighter, broader, and higher. However, this power is only a force that helps everything become joyful and supports joy in the path of love. There lies all the absolute authority that God possesses, as well as eternity and infinitude. It does not aim to restrict the path of love or apply brakes. It serves only as a stimulating element to transcend time and space and unify, not as a hindrance. In such a position, how happy would humans be to receive God's love?

From this perspective, historically, if there was a man who received such love among our fathers, grandfathers, or human ancestors, that man would be worthy of pride. If there was a representative woman who received such love, even if the man did not, that woman would also be worthy of pride. When viewed this way, that love is not temporary but eternal. Is that not so?

Even in this fallen world, when lovers live their lives centered around the promises they made to each other, even if they live in solitude, when we see people who pursue that love and live according to the inner emotional connections of that love, the stimulation felt centered around God's love in the original world that has not fallen, in the ideal world that has been completed, is not temporary but eternal. Because that stimulation of love is eternal, its beginning would have become a tradition, and that tradition would have become the subject of power that could lead history in one direction. When viewed this way, has there been anyone who has received such love from God? There has not.

The highest hope that believers desire today
So what should be the highest hope that we believers desire today? It should be a higher love. It is not some power. It is not knowledge. Of course, we must pursue truth, but truth is not the fundamental issue. Love is needed first, and then truth comes. Isn't that right? After being happy, knowledge is needed; if one is unhappy, what good is knowledge? If one is unhappy, what good is power? If one is unhappy, what good is money? If a loved one is about to die, what good is money?

When we look at it this way, everything is about what is needed, but fundamentally, after leaving behind the love one desires, after establishing love as the primary condition, only then are additional conditions necessary. Power, knowledge, and money are all supplementary conditions.

Living is the same. What does it mean to live as a human? What does it mean to live like an animal? That is why the path of a loved one is one that one wants to follow even after death. Therefore, even if there are countless desires to live, eat, possess, and do something, those are all needed after having love; if one loses love, are they not all unnecessary? Is that not so? After losing love, do we not feel disheartened? Is that not true?

When we think about it this way, what kind of being is God? God is the subject of love. If God is the subject of love, then He must be higher than us humans, mustn't He? If we are humans, then He must be greater than us. He is absolutely greater.

From this perspective, what kind of person would the one whom He longs for, the one He wants to see, the one He loves madly, be? Think about it. When I become the subject of His love and receive His love, no one in this world can dominate me. Only absolute love can be my motivation, my process, and my result; everything else cannot follow me anywhere. There must be a model centered around such a human. There must be a man and a woman of such a model. When viewed from this principle, the term fall is extremely miserable. Regardless of what happened, the very term fall, the notion of incompleteness and failure to fulfill purpose, is miserable. Who is it miserable for? It is not miserable for us humans; it is miserable for God.

Humans made God, who was already miserable, even more miserable.
Today, general believers who believe in God praise Him as the omniscient, omnipotent, and absolute God, hoping to find happiness through Him. But has He truly become the God who can give us happiness in the true sense?

When you are unhappy, do you not get irritated? Do you not? Even if you are told not to be irritated, you still are. Your hands get irritated, your eyes get irritated, and your entire body gets irritated. It is the same for the body as it is for the heart.

From this perspective, when one approaches God, who has lost the highest ideal counterpart, wearing the rags of all sins, and says, "Father God! Please take my sins. God, I have committed such and such sins. Please take my sins," if God can only respond, "Okay," how miserable must He be? How pitiful must He be? Can that be happiness?
for the sake of the ideal of love that God desires, and the path of faith that we must walk. 

In this context, when we think about the suffering that God has endured, we must understand that God has not yet fully experienced the love of a man in the truest sense. God has not had the opportunity to love a man in the way that He desires. Therefore, the historical process is a search for that ideal man, the Messiah, who can fulfill God's longing for love and establish the ideal relationship between God and humanity.

The Messiah is not just a figure of history but the embodiment of God's hope and desire. The Messiah represents the culmination of God's efforts to restore humanity and create a world where His love can be fully realized. This is why the concept of the Messiah is so significant in religious thought, as it encapsulates the ultimate goal of human existence and the divine plan.

In conclusion, the journey of faith is not merely about individual salvation or personal fulfillment; it is about participating in the larger narrative of God's love and the restoration of the world. Each believer is called to contribute to this divine purpose, understanding that their struggles and sacrifices are part of a greater plan that transcends individual experiences. The path of faith is a collective journey toward the realization of God's ideal, where love, unity, and harmony can flourish in the world.
It is. Isn't it?  
The Messiah who comes as a representative to complete God's love  
Fortunately, there is a religion on this earth, and that religion has the belief in the Second Coming, which states that at the end of times, a man who can serve as a model for humanity will emerge. This has remained a hope throughout the history of human sorrow.  
When the owner of that hope reigns, what should he bring? He is not someone who brings money. He is not someone who brings power. He is not someone who brings knowledge. Those are all secondary conditions. He comes as a representative of a man who can complete the noble love of God above all else. He comes as the substantial object of God's love. Only he can pursue completion, and only he can determine completion as a subjective representative. Has there ever been such a person in human history? That is why history has been searching for that one man until now. This is the conclusion of the belief in the Second Coming in religion.  
So what will God pursue? Not money, not knowledge, not power. God does not need such things. However, the one absolute God needs love. Therefore, a world without the object of love is a world like darkness. It is a world like a desert, a world like a glacier. God does not want such a world. That is why He seeks a world of hope beyond a world like death. This has been the providential history until now.  
Then, if He comes to this earth, what should we learn from Him and inherit as tradition? It is not money. It is not power. It is not any kind of skill. It is not any kind of knowledge. The issue is how to excavate the hidden love of God.  
When that love becomes three-dimensional, and when we stand in a position to pursue the relative value that God desires, then God can be pleased. That joy must begin from God for me to be able to rejoice. I cannot be happy while God is sad.  
You say that God is pleased when you repent of your sins, right? What is the reason for His joy? It is because a bridge can be built to pave the way for restoration. It is not that He rejoices because an ideal has been realized. The primary desire is for that foundation, so He rejoices, but the secondary desire is not for that foundation, but for the ideal of love that can remain on that foundation forever. Everyone must understand that.  
So what should the members of the Unification Church long for? The ideal love that God wants to govern. What kind of love is God's love? It is the combination of parental love, spousal love, and children's love all at once. If that does not feel real…  
Those who have learned the Principle know that we humans did not start from receiving God's love. Whose love did we start from? We started from the love of Satan, who became the enemy of God due to the fall. What kind of being is Satan? He is below Adam. Of course, he is below God, and he is a being below Adam's son. In other words, we started from the origin of the love of a servant, which is the fallen human world today. Do you understand what I mean?  
The emotional foundation of humanity until now, what has it been? It has not been God's love, but Satan's love.  
What is Satan? He is the archangel. The love of that archangel can only be called a love of rebirth. If we call the archangelic love rebirth, then Adamic love is a love of growth, and God's love is completion. Therefore, we must go through rebirth, growth, and completion. This is how we see it. However, fallen humans are born within the realm of Satan's love and struggle to live based on that foundation. Do you understand? What does Satan's love deny? It denies the position of humanity. It denies the position of Adam and Eve and denies the position of God.  
Because we started from the historical tradition of the realm of Satan, when we look at the history of humanity, humans have become beings that deny human value. They have become people who do not even know what human value is. They have become people who do not even know whether God exists or not.  
God's love cannot be understood through explanation.  
If we had originally become one with the absolute love of God, there would be no need for explanations about what love is. Can you explain to young men and women, "This is what love is"? Do they understand? Can an orphan understand what parental love is, no matter how many times you explain it? They can only understand what parental love is when they have children of their own. Before that, they do not know. They just think, "It seems like that." Does "seems like that" match with "is"? What seems like that can be completely opposite. In true meaning, the love that says "this is love"…  
Humans did not start from the ideal love realm centered on God, but from the position of the love of the archangel. Therefore, no matter how many theories we establish and come to conclusions, the motivation that made humans like this can only be the love of the archangel.  
The love of the archangel can also sacrifice life. In the world, we often see parents sacrificing their lives for their children, right? But knowing the higher value of the original human being and knowing and loving the subject God, can we talk about whether God exists or not? Can we discuss whether God exists or not? Such discussions are the actions of a fool, an abnormal person.  
Can someone who has experienced God's love say that God does not exist? The subject and the object have both experienced love, and they have felt what love is, but can they still say that it does not exist? If the sensory organs have felt the strongest consciousness, what can deny that? Because there is nothing to deny, God absolutely exists. Therefore, there is no need to think about whether God exists or not.  
When humans come into contact with God's love…  
You breathe, but do you count the number of breaths? Do you hear the sound of your heart beating like a hammer in your chest? You can feel a fly lightly touch your hair, but you do not feel the hammer pounding your heart. Isn't that strange? You know when a fly passes by, but you do not know when your heart is pounding like a hammer. So that is harmony.  
If you were to count the sound of your heartbeat, you would all become neurotic. One, two, three, four… Can you count like that? Have you ever thought about your heart beating for a day, a week, ten days, or a month? If you were to look at it relatively, it would be a big problem. Look! Today it goes like this, and tomorrow it goes slightly like that, and if you think like that, you would die. So it is good that you do not know. If you were to look at it relatively, it would be a big problem.  
Everyone, it is good that the nerve organs in our bodies are not visible. Imagine if there were spiderweb-like nerves that you could see working. It is so complex… If we were to say it is a machine, it is the most precise machine. There are millions of parts, and can we say that it does not break down? When we see it this way, it is good that we cannot see it all; if we could see it, it would be a big problem. It is good that we do not know that our hearts are beating; knowing it would be a big problem.  
Why do we not know? Because it is too close. Because it is above our life… That is why. It is not just the sense of life that I exist in; it is because it is within me. It acts as a wall, and it must be reflected like a movie screen, and because it is transcending that wall, we do not know it until we go around that wall.  
God is the same. God is not visible because He is too close. Our eyes are also close, so they do not see. Therefore, whether it is close or far, it does not appear, right? Everything in the world is like that. That is why for those who have felt love with God, the question of whether God exists or not does not matter. Isn't that right? There is such a world.  
Then, if even the love of the archangel can lead to life and death struggles, how much more so would Adamic love be? What would Adamic love be like? If you pour cold water into boiling water or throw in ice, what happens? Does it make a sound or not? It makes a loud sound. Try it. "Oh, it feels good to have cold water come in when it is hot." It explodes. Do you understand? That love has hundreds of trillions of cells rushing in all at once. Do you understand?  
But what happens if you come into contact with God's love? Your hair dances, and your cells dance. That is right. If you are 100% intoxicated by that love, it is not that you fall down; it becomes eternal life. If someone tries to wake you up, you would say not to wake up. A mystical world unfolds. There is a saying that in the joy of the divine, the handle of the axe rots, right? There must be a way to be intoxicated by a love that is so high that humans cannot imagine it.  
Humans must live in a state of intoxication. A person who lives in intoxication is a happy person. Artists live in intoxication with their art. Those who engage in literature write books they envision or live in intoxication with some masterpiece. Such people are happy. Therefore, the whole body of humanity must be intoxicated with the three-dimensional ideal love of God and follow Him alone. However, because humans have lost that love, they externally connect pipes to drink alcohol and become intoxicated, or they take opium to get high. Is God's love worse than opium? Is God's love worse than alcohol? Is God's love worse than honey? They call the things of the world of Satan, like a dog, love, and they struggle to live and die with that, and they talk about how love is eternal, but think about it.  
If someone has felt God's love, that person will automatically dance rhythmically before anyone teaches them to dance. Just push the button… If you match the frequency, like an unmanned aircraft coming in when it is called, they will play along as it goes, and they will not say, "I don't like it!" and fall away.  
Yet, do you still have thoughts about whether God exists or not? Discussing whether God exists or not is the act of a madman; it is abnormal. It is like saying, "I have no husband, what is a husband's love?" even though you have a husband.  
The way to reach heaven is…  
So what is God's desire? Is it that you all give birth to many sons and daughters and dance happily? If you dance happily seeing those sons and daughters, that is only the dance of the world of Satan. It is because they were born from a false love that the false love must be resolved. From this perspective, Jesus also set the standard by saying, "If you do not love me more than anyone else, you are not worthy of me." Two thousand years ago, Jesus said, "Anyone who does not love me more than their mother, father, wife, or children is not worthy of me." He said they were not worthy to be disciples. Moreover, He said, "Take up your cross and follow me."  
Until now, in the historical age, humans have only sought to do well for themselves. If that is the case, everyone will perish. Therefore, what is the secret to salvation? It is to say, "I am a pitiful person, but how pitiful is God, who treats me, a pitiful person? That pitiful God must save a world where pitiful people like me live, and since I am already a sinful being destined to perish, if I can die in place of the sins of the people of the world and forgive them, then please forgive me." This is the only way. This is the way of religion, the way of the cross, and it must be clearly understood.  
Since there is no other way for me to find heaven than to bear God's burden and lessen the path of God's labor, Jesus stood as a representative in the position of sacrificing himself and praying for the blessings of his enemies. There is no other way to leave the thought of goodness in a world of disbelief.  
We must feel God's love in the emotional realm. We must excavate God's love once again. Then, do we not have such elements in our own nature? There are plenty of elements. When you look at a compass, if you place iron filings on a board and bring a magnet close to it, the iron filings will follow along. Even if you say, "Hey, do not come," they will come along. If you raise it high, it weakens gradually. If it rises too high, it becomes vague. We humans are like this. We have been separated for 6,000 years. The 6,000 years in the Bible could be tens of thousands of years. There are also claims that human history is 80 million years long…  
God is like a magnet, and humans are like iron. When God moves back and forth like this, the tip of the iron moves along. Do you understand? Still, your ancestors who were good people move a bit more at the top. Depending on the weight, if the ancestor is a better ancestor, the bottom will move as well. It is like an antenna.  
Humans have such a nature. That is why we must excavate such a nature. To do that, we must strip away. What must we strip away? We must strip away the shells of tradition, habits, history, culture, ideology, and background. This ragged shell clings to us. So if you want to see with your eyes, take it off. If you want to eat, then take it off. If you want to smell, then take it off. If you want to taste, then take it off. You must deny everything. If you deny everything, everything disappears. Then you must be intoxicated with God's love and call Him Father. Then it will stick to you. That is what I mean.  
Only then will the justification of all religions until now stand. Have you sought a non-existent God like that? If so, religion is something that cannot be accepted in the human world… What should we call this? Deception, deception. That is why now there is a term called "development of the heart." It means to develop the field of the heart. There are many rocky fields, many thorny bushes, many boulders, many valleys, and many rugged mountains, and it is said to make this into a flat land.  
What is that heart? What is drawn in the heart is love, but we do not even know whether it is love or not. The fastest way from here is the way of love. The fastest way is the way of love. Therefore, you must develop that. You must know that.  
From this perspective, what believers must always be careful of is that believers must be taught. They will be taught through hints, dreams, revelations, or visions. A hint is something that comes from unrelated places; for example, a fly flies by here, and something is associated with it, leading to realization.
is what we are doing. We must live centered on God's love. This is the essence of our faith and our purpose. 

We need to understand that God's love is not just a concept but a reality that we must experience and embody in our lives. When we truly feel God's love, it transforms us and guides our actions. 

In order to love God, we must first understand what it means to be loved by Him. This means recognizing our worth as His children and embracing the identity that comes with that. We are not just individuals; we are part of a greater family, a divine lineage that connects us to each other and to God.

As we strive to live in accordance with God's love, we must also be aware of the responsibilities that come with it. Love is not passive; it requires action, commitment, and sacrifice. We must be willing to put in the effort to cultivate our relationship with God and with one another.

In our daily lives, we should seek to express God's love through our words and deeds. This means being compassionate, understanding, and supportive of those around us. It also means standing up for what is right and just, even when it is difficult.

Ultimately, our goal is to create a world where God's love reigns supreme. This is not just a dream; it is a calling that we must answer with our lives. We are the instruments through which God's love can be made manifest in the world.

So let us commit ourselves to this path, to live as true children of God, and to share His love with everyone we encounter. In doing so, we will not only fulfill our purpose but also bring joy and hope to a world that so desperately needs it.
In order for this world to come under God's dominion, for this nation to be embraced within God's love... we are to pave the way of tears. We are to pave the highway. Wasn't there a sacrifice of 77 people in the construction of the Gyeongbu Expressway? What I am grateful for is how much the Unification Church has sacrificed in paving the path of heaven's providence. I myself have not yet sacrificed, although I have endured some hardships... True filial piety emerges only after one sacrifices their life, and true loyalty appears only after one gives their life. No matter how much hardship one has endured for 70 or 80 years, they cannot compare to a young loyalist who has sacrificed their life. From this perspective, you must understand that because there was no such sacrifice, God has paid the price of sacrifice. You must realize that while you are asleep, God is engaged in a fierce battle. 

Therefore, you should hold hands, connect army to army, district to district, village to village, family to family. By reaching out to individuals, connecting the 3,000 ri peninsula from Seoul, we can expand the ideal dominion where we can hold and serve God's hand. Isn't this the restoration of God's world? From this standpoint, haven't you been called by God? 

Today, you are not alone. You must understand how urgent this time is. Considering the countless battles this nation must face, we must center ourselves on God's love, embrace it, and pray. We must love our nation and love the world. You must know that only by introducing God's love and establishing and developing the environment of God's dominion, the connections of God's love, can this world be under God's dominion. I have shared this in hopes that you will live this way.

<Prayer> Father, before your love, I am an exceedingly foolish being. Standing here, I seem ignorant and have lived foolishly. Even while possessing the features of the world, I could not manage myself, forgetting everything to fight only for you. When I think about how difficult that path is, how much pain your heart must have felt in asking me to walk that path. How sorrowful must your heart have been to have to place me in such a position? 

That one heart has become the driving force of life, allowing me to stand here today without dying and to face the young children. I deeply feel that this is only possible on the foundation of your hard work and effort. Father, when I think about the insignificant things I have established and the great promises, I am humbled. It is pitiful that there is no one who can believe, and you, wanting to hold onto these people, are to be pitied. It is sad that there is no nation to seek, and you have come to find this pitiful Korean people.

There are many countries in the world that are more capable than this nation. There are many who are superior to us in calling your name. However, I have come to know that before your love, they are distant. When I see a foolish and innocent child longing only for their parents and crying, it may seem foolish at first glance, but when I think about the deep longing that comes from the bones, wanting to embrace and weep, I realize how many times I have felt that way.

No matter what the world says, I have fought until today because you were there. No matter what the nation says, I am carefully walking this path, fearing that it may obscure your glory. Some may say that the leaders of the Unification Church are happy, but the path of love has been a difficult one. I know that the path of filial piety is not one to boast about after walking it. I have come to understand that the path of a loyalist is one that feels shame after doing all they can.

Father, if there is to be a day when the person called the Unification Church can hold their head high and boast, you know well that it is only after you can do so first that I wish to do so. We must go and go, run and run. We must go at night and go during the day. Even if we are tired, we must go, and even if we collapse from exhaustion, we must go. I know that this path, which must be lived with a fate that leaves behind regrets even in the face of death, is a happier path, and I am grateful for having fought until this day.

Father, I know that your desire is to govern the world. To achieve that world, one must even sacrifice their own kin. To establish that world, we must walk the unjust path of sacrificing the beloved members of the Unification Church. I understand that to realize the world under heaven's dominion, we must walk the path of sacrificing countless religious people. I know that to achieve the world of heaven, we must even sacrifice South Korea to save the world.

Some people say that the Unification Church dreams of seizing earthly power. No, we are a group that longs for your nation of love. You know that we are a group that has no attachment to the world. 

When the thirty million people are united before your love, Kim Il-sung is not the problem. The Communist Party is not the problem. The ideology that denies God, this non-principled and non-truthful thought is not the problem. It is not a matter of a million words; it is a matter of the experiences I hold that cannot be denied, no matter what anyone says. There is no logic to deny a mother who loves you, no logic to deny a wife who loves you, and no logic to deny a child who loves you. This is the problem. I have come to understand that being a son, daughter, and master who can dwell in your house is the issue. I earnestly hope and wish to become such children.

This morning, your sons and daughters here are now sending off July. As we welcome August, may the time of your hope draw near. May the day come quickly when this nation of North and South Korea, which must resolve the tragic history, can look upon the radiant light of your love. 

For this, we must go again. We have shed blood and sweat to walk the path of persecution in South Korea, but we must also fight to walk the path of persecution in North Korea. Now is the time when the members of the Unification Church must resolve to cross the borders of the nation or they cannot remain as members of the Unification Church.

Father! I hope that your people, who can overcome life and death to love heaven, will be such. I know that the August we must welcome can be a month to boast of liberation and independence. 

When I think about the first liberation from Japanese colonial rule, the second liberation that must break down the barriers between North and South, and the third liberation that must break down the barriers of the world, I realize that this is the path of the Unification Church. We are a group that must not die without seeing the day when we achieve this third liberation of the world and you become the victorious sovereign and the leader of love.

Father, we have such circumstances, so I hope and wish that you will guide and be with us. I earnestly ask and wish to start as such a group, remain as such a group, and end as such a group. 

May your love and compassion be upon our insignificant heads, our lives, and our existence forever. I earnestly request this, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
